# Integración de GitHub - Manus Documentation

[Saltar al contenido principal](https://manus.im/docs/es/website-builder/github-integration#content-area)

[Manus Documentation home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/docs-manus/C1PisAhqAuyVufRp/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=C1PisAhqAuyVufRp&q=85&s=7366a98aefb64c7c37c7dd35d613c640)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/docs-manus/C1PisAhqAuyVufRp/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=C1PisAhqAuyVufRp&q=85&s=1b58c59477c90d5dbf1454f25864b789)](https://manus.im/docs)

![ES](https://d3gk2c5xim1je2.cloudfront.net/flags/ES.svg)

Español

Buscar...

⌘K

Buscar...

Navigation

Herramientas para Desarrolladores

Integración de GitHub

[Introducción](https://manus.im/docs/es/introduction/welcome)
[Características](https://manus.im/docs/es/features/design-view)
[Constructor de Sitios Web](https://manus.im/docs/es/website-builder/getting-started)
[Integraciones](https://manus.im/docs/es/integrations/integrations)

En esta página

*   [Conecte su proyecto Manus a GitHub](https://manus.im/docs/es/website-builder/github-integration#conecte-su-proyecto-manus-a-github)
    
*   [Cómo Usarlo](https://manus.im/docs/es/website-builder/github-integration#c%C3%B3mo-usarlo)
    
*   [Lo Que Necesita Saber](https://manus.im/docs/es/website-builder/github-integration#lo-que-necesita-saber)
    
*   [Capacidades del Conector de GitHub](https://manus.im/docs/es/website-builder/github-integration#capacidades-del-conector-de-github)
    
*   [Desconexión de la Integración](https://manus.im/docs/es/website-builder/github-integration#desconexi%C3%B3n-de-la-integraci%C3%B3n)
    
*   [Preguntas Frecuentes](https://manus.im/docs/es/website-builder/github-integration#preguntas-frecuentes)
    

Piense en GitHub como un servicio basado en la nube para almacenar y gestionar código. Al igual que usted podría usar Google Docs para escribir y guardar documentos en línea, los desarrolladores usan GitHub para guardar su código, rastrear cambios a lo largo del tiempo y colaborar con otros. Cada proyecto en GitHub se almacena en un repositorio, que es como una carpeta para su proyecto. Dentro, puede encontrar todos los archivos de código y un historial completo de cada cambio que se ha realizado. Esto lo convierte en una herramienta poderosa para el control de versiones y el trabajo en equipo en el desarrollo de software.

[​](https://manus.im/docs/es/website-builder/github-integration#conecte-su-proyecto-manus-a-github)

Conecte su proyecto Manus a GitHub
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![Untitled Design (2)](https://mintcdn.com/docs-manus/OMZXVO9ke2Xqfh0m/images/Untitleddesign(2).jpg?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=OMZXVO9ke2Xqfh0m&q=85&s=1de5acab156fd0924458adf7094acf98) La Integración de GitHub le permite exportar el código de su proyecto Manus a un nuevo repositorio privado de GitHub. Una vez exportado, se establece una sincronización bidireccional entre su espacio de trabajo Manus y el repositorio de GitHub. ![Screenshot 2025 12 26 At 5 55 39 PM](https://mintcdn.com/docs-manus/OMZXVO9ke2Xqfh0m/images/Screenshot2025-12-26at5.55.39PM.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=OMZXVO9ke2Xqfh0m&q=85&s=65cb5b1c1ff0258cf51d41f5dff9692d) Esto le ofrece lo mejor de ambos mundos: el poder del desarrollo impulsado por AI en Manus y la flexibilidad de trabajar en su código en su propio entorno.

[​](https://manus.im/docs/es/website-builder/github-integration#c%C3%B3mo-usarlo)

Cómo Usarlo
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Autorización: En el panel de control de su proyecto, haga clic en el icono de GitHub en la esquina superior derecha o navegue a la pestaña de GitHub en Configuración. Si no ha conectado su cuenta de GitHub antes, se le pedirá que autorice la conexión.
2.  Exportar a un Nuevo Repositorio: Una vez que su cuenta esté conectada, elija un propietario (usted o una organización a la que pertenezca) y un nombre para el nuevo repositorio antes de hacer clic en “Crear Repositorio”. Esta acción crea un nuevo repositorio privado en su cuenta de GitHub que contiene todo el código de su proyecto. A Manus se le otorgan automáticamente los permisos necesarios para sincronizarse con este nuevo repositorio.

Advertencia: Cambiar el propietario o el nombre del repositorio en GitHub después de que haya sido creado romperá la conexión con Manus.

1.  Sincronice su Código: Con el repositorio creado, Manus mantiene su proyecto y la rama principal de su repositorio de GitHub sincronizados automáticamente.

*   Envío Automático: Cuando Manus genera o modifica código en su proyecto, los cambios se envían automáticamente a la rama principal.
*   Extracción Automática: Antes de realizar cualquier cambio de código nuevo, Manus extrae primero la última versión de la rama principal para reducir el riesgo de conflictos.
*   Sincronización Manual & Verificación de Estado: Puede verificar el estado de sincronización en cualquier momento haciendo clic en el icono de GitHub. Desde allí, también puede activar manualmente una extracción para asegurarse de que su proyecto Manus esté actualizado con cualquier cambio que haya realizado directamente en GitHub.

[​](https://manus.im/docs/es/website-builder/github-integration#lo-que-necesita-saber)

Lo Que Necesita Saber
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Una vez que su código está en GitHub, usted tiene control total. Puede clonar el repositorio en su máquina local, realizar ediciones en su IDE favorito y enviar sus cambios de vuelta a la rama principal en GitHub. Cuando regrese a Manus, extraerá esas actualizaciones antes de realizar su siguiente conjunto de cambios, lo que ayuda a mantener su trabajo sincronizado y reduce las posibilidades de sobrescribir sus ediciones manuales. Consejo: Use Manus para generar la estructura y el código base inicial para su aplicación. Luego, exporte su código a GitHub y use su IDE favorito para los toques finales y la implementación detallada. Una vez que esté listo, sincronice su trabajo de vuelta a Manus para una fácil implementación y alojamiento.

[​](https://manus.im/docs/es/website-builder/github-integration#capacidades-del-conector-de-github)

Capacidades del Conector de GitHub
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Conectar su proyecto a GitHub también activa el Conector de GitHub, lo que le da a Manus la capacidad de ayudarle a gestionar su repositorio directamente desde la interfaz de Manus. Los permisos otorgados permiten a Manus realizar varias acciones comunes en su nombre:

*   Gestionar Código: Leer y escribir código, confirmar cambios y manejar operaciones de push/pull para mantener su repositorio sincronizado.
*   Gestionar Problemas: Crear, ver, editar y cerrar problemas en su repositorio.
*   Trabajar con Solicitudes de Extracción: Crear, ver, editar y cerrar solicitudes de extracción.
*   Organizar Proyectos: Interactuar con los tableros de proyecto de su repositorio.

Estas capacidades permiten un flujo de trabajo más integrado, donde puede gestionar su ciclo de vida de desarrollo sin cambiar constantemente entre Manus y GitHub.

[​](https://manus.im/docs/es/website-builder/github-integration#desconexi%C3%B3n-de-la-integraci%C3%B3n)

Desconexión de la Integración
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Si desea dejar de sincronizar su proyecto con GitHub, puede desconectar la integración desde la configuración de su proyecto. La desconexión no eliminará su repositorio de GitHub; simplemente evita que Manus envíe o extraiga más cambios. Conservará la propiedad total del repositorio en GitHub, pero su proyecto Manus ya no estará conectado a él.

[​](https://manus.im/docs/es/website-builder/github-integration#preguntas-frecuentes)

Preguntas Frecuentes
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

¿Qué debo hacer si recibo un error de "autorización de GitHub fallida"?

Este error puede ocurrir por dos razones principales:

1.  Su conexión necesita ser actualizada. Para resolver esto, vaya a la configuración de su proyecto, desconecte su cuenta de GitHub y luego vuelva a conectarla.
2.  Manus no tiene permiso para acceder al repositorio. Esto puede suceder si está intentando sincronizarse con un repositorio que no fue creado originalmente a través de la función de exportación de Manus, o si el nombre o el propietario del repositorio se cambiaron después de la creación. Asegúrese de estar trabajando con el repositorio que Manus creó para su proyecto bajo su nombre y propietario originales.

[Integraciones de Terceros](https://manus.im/docs/es/website-builder/third-party-integrations)

⌘I

Manus API

[Introduction](https://manus.im/docs/introduction/welcome)
[Features](https://manus.im/docs/features/design-view)

On this page

*   [What is the Manus API?](https://manus.im/docs/integrations/manus-api#what-is-the-manus-api)
    
*   [Why Use the Manus API?](https://manus.im/docs/integrations/manus-api#why-use-the-manus-api)
    

[​](https://manus.im/docs/integrations/manus-api#what-is-the-manus-api)

What is the Manus API?
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Manus API is a RESTful API that allows developers to integrate Manus directly into their applications, workflows, and systems. Instead of using Manus through the web interface or mobile app, you can trigger tasks, manage files, and receive results programmatically. This enables you to embed Manus’s complete AI agent capabilities—research, analysis, content creation, data processing, and more—into your own products and workflows.

[​](https://manus.im/docs/integrations/manus-api#why-use-the-manus-api)

Why Use the Manus API?
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Most AI APIs provide narrow capabilities: text generation, image analysis, or specific tasks. The Manus API gives you access to a complete AI agent that can plan, execute multi-step workflows, use tools, browse the web, and deliver results in multiple formats. **Traditional AI APIs**: Call an endpoint, get a text response. **Manus API**: Send a task, Manus plans the approach, gathers information, uses tools, and delivers complete results (reports, presentations, websites, data analysis, etc.). This transforms how you can integrate AI into your applications—from simple text generation to autonomous task completion. **Next steps**: [View the complete API reference](https://open.manus.im/docs)

[​](https://manus.im/docs/integrations/manus-browser-operator#what-is-manus-browser-operator)

What is Manus Browser Operator?
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Manus Browser Operator is a browser extension that enables Manus to operate directly within your local browser environment. Unlike the cloud browser that Manus typically uses, Browser Operator works with your actual browser—complete with your existing logins, sessions, and local IP address. This transforms your browser from a passive viewing tool into an active workspace where Manus can execute complex tasks using the premium tools and authenticated systems you already access.

[​](https://manus.im/docs/integrations/manus-browser-operator#why-local-browser-matters)

Why Local Browser Matters
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/integrations/manus-browser-operator#the-authentication-advantage)

The Authentication Advantage

When Manus works in your local browser, it operates with your trusted credentials and local IP address. This means: **No Login Barriers**: The system recognizes activity as coming from your trusted machine, eliminating unfamiliar login attempts, CAPTCHA interruptions, and session expiration issues. **Reliable Access**: Because the activity appears legitimate to websites, it clears standard access barriers automatically and maintains active sessions. **Premium Tool Access**: Manus can work with subscription services you’re already logged into—Crunchbase, PitchBook, SimilarWeb, Financial Times, Semrush, Ahrefs, or any authenticated platform.

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/integrations/manus-browser-operator#cloud-browser-vs-local-browser)

Cloud Browser vs. Local Browser

**Cloud Browser** (Default):

*   Sandboxed, isolated environment
*   Works across any device without installation
*   Ideal for most research, analysis, and content creation tasks
*   No local setup required

**Local Browser** (Browser Operator):

*   Uses your actual browser with existing sessions
*   Access to authenticated systems and premium tools
*   Trusted local IP and credentials
*   Best for workflows requiring logged-in access

Both work together seamlessly—Manus automatically uses the appropriate environment for each task.

[​](https://manus.im/docs/integrations/manus-browser-operator#how-it-works)

How It Works
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/integrations/manus-browser-operator#3-step-process)

3-Step Process

**Step 1: Activate “My Browser” Connector** Navigate to Connectors and toggle on “My Browser.” This tells Manus to use your local browser for tasks requiring web access. **Step 2: Authorize the Session** When you assign a task, Manus requests permission to take control. Click “Authorize” to grant one-time access. You remain in command of when and how Manus interacts with your browser. **Step 3: Monitor in Dedicated Tab** Manus opens a new tab within a tab group named after your current task. You can:

*   Watch the task unfold in real-time
*   Take over by clicking into the tab
*   Stop instantly by closing the tab

[​](https://manus.im/docs/integrations/manus-browser-operator#real-world-use-cases)

Real-World Use Cases
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/integrations/manus-browser-operator#market-research-with-premium-tools)

Market Research with Premium Tools

**Scenario**: Analyze 20 competitors using your Crunchbase and PitchBook subscriptions **Without Browser Operator**: Manual login, navigation, data extraction, and compilation across multiple platforms **With Browser Operator**: **Result**: Manus accesses both platforms using your authenticated sessions, extracts data systematically, and delivers a comprehensive comparison table.

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/integrations/manus-browser-operator#seo-analysis-at-scale)

SEO Analysis at Scale

**Scenario**: Audit 50 competitor websites using your Semrush and Ahrefs accounts **Request**: **Result**: Automated analysis across both premium SEO tools with your subscription access, delivering actionable insights.

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/integrations/manus-browser-operator#crm-data-enrichment)

CRM Data Enrichment

**Scenario**: Enrich 100 leads in your CRM with additional research **Request**: **Result**: Systematic enrichment using your authenticated access to premium B2B tools.

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/integrations/manus-browser-operator#financial-research)

Financial Research

**Scenario**: Compile market intelligence from paywalled sources **Request**: **Result**: Comprehensive research synthesis from premium financial sources you’re subscribed to.

[​](https://manus.im/docs/integrations/manus-browser-operator#transparency-and-control)

Transparency and Control
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/integrations/manus-browser-operator#full-visibility)

Full Visibility

Every action Manus takes is meticulously logged, providing a clear audit trail. You can see exactly what Manus is doing at each step.

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/integrations/manus-browser-operator#instant-stop)

Instant Stop

If you need to halt a task immediately, simply close the dedicated tab. Manus stops instantly.

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/integrations/manus-browser-operator#remote-access)

Remote Access

Because Manus operates locally within your desktop browser, you can initiate and monitor tasks from your phone or another device. As long as your primary computer is online, your AI assistant is ready to work from anywhere.

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/integrations/manus-browser-operator#review-before-authorization)

Review Before Authorization

If a site contains sensitive information, you can review what Manus will access before clicking “Authorize.” You always maintain control.

[​](https://manus.im/docs/integrations/manus-browser-operator#availability-and-compatibility)

Availability and Compatibility
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Current Status**: Beta rollout to Pro, Plus, and Team users **Supported Browsers**:

*   Chrome (recommended)
*   Edge (recommended)
*   Additional browsers coming soon

**Current Limitations**:

*   Complex interactions (drag-and-drop, multi-step forms) may not work perfectly
*   Some websites with aggressive anti-bot measures may require manual intervention

[​](https://manus.im/docs/integrations/manus-browser-operator#security-and-privacy)

Security and Privacy
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/integrations/manus-browser-operator#your-control)

Your Control

*   **One-time authorization**: Each task requires explicit permission
*   **Visible activity**: All actions logged and visible in real-time
*   **Instant termination**: Close tab to stop immediately
*   **Selective access**: Choose which tasks use local browser

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/integrations/manus-browser-operator#your-data)

Your Data

*   Manus operates within your browser using your existing sessions
*   No credentials are stored or transmitted
*   Activity appears as coming from your local machine
*   Standard Manus privacy policies apply

[​](https://manus.im/docs/integrations/manus-browser-operator#tips-for-best-results)

Tips for Best Results
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Be specific about tool usage**:

*   ✅ “Use my Crunchbase account to research these companies”
*   ❌ “Research these companies”

**Verify logins first**:

*   Ensure you’re logged into required services before starting task
*   Check that sessions are active and not expired

**Review sensitive sites**:

*   Before authorizing, confirm which sites Manus will access
*   Use caution with financial accounts or sensitive data

**Monitor first few tasks**:

*   Watch initial tasks to understand how Browser Operator works
*   Adjust prompts based on observed behavior

**Combine with other features**:

*   Use Wide Research for parallel processing across multiple items
*   Export results to slides, reports, or structured data

[​](https://manus.im/docs/integrations/manus-browser-operator#common-questions)

Common Questions
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Does Browser Operator work on mobile?

You can initiate tasks from mobile, but your desktop browser must be running for Browser Operator to function.

Is my login information safe

Manus doesn’t store or transmit your credentials. It operates within your existing browser sessions.

Can I revoke access mid-task?

Yes. Close the dedicated tab to stop Manus immediately.

[​](https://manus.im/docs/integrations/nano-banana-pro#what-is-nano-banana-pro)

What is Nano Banana Pro?
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Nano Banana Pro is Google’s advanced image generation model, integrated directly into Manus for creating professional-quality visuals. When you need slides or images that look like they were designed by a studio, Nano Banana Pro generates custom, high-resolution imagery tailored specifically to your content. This transforms Manus from a text-based tool into a complete visual content creation platform, capable of producing presentation decks and graphics that would typically require professional design software and expertise.

[​](https://manus.im/docs/integrations/nano-banana-pro#why-use-nano-banana-pro)

Why Use Nano Banana Pro?
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Most AI image generators struggle with two critical problems: they can’t render readable text within images, and they can’t maintain visual consistency across multiple outputs. This makes them impractical for professional presentations. Nano Banana Pro solves both:

*   Nano Banana’s text rendering: Crisp, legible text integrated directly into images
*   Manus’s contextual understanding: Consistent artistic direction across entire decks

This enables professional-quality visual content without design skills or expensive software

[​](https://manus.im/docs/integrations/nano-banana-pro#getting-started-with-nano-banana-pro)

Getting Started with Nano Banana Pro
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/integrations/nano-banana-pro#for-slide-decks)

For Slide Decks

1.  Open Manus and navigate to the Slides section ![Screenshot 2025-12-08 at 11.52.12 AM.png](https://mintcdn.com/docs-manus/SsKP6I-rYVXzKghN/images/Screenshot2025-12-08at11.52.12AM.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=SsKP6I-rYVXzKghN&q=85&s=dba068475f315df8860ae58382d08d51)
2.  Look for templates marked with the 🍌 Nano Banana icon OR just write your prompt ![Screenshot 2025-12-08 at 11.51.28 AM.png](https://mintcdn.com/docs-manus/SsKP6I-rYVXzKghN/images/Screenshot2025-12-08at11.51.28AM.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=SsKP6I-rYVXzKghN&q=85&s=16cfe65d8b5cda36af7396a4eab706b1)
3.  Write your prompt describing your presentation topic and desired style
4.  Select slide count (typically 8-12 slides)
5.  Generate and wait for your deck to be created (2-5 minutes)

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/integrations/nano-banana-pro#for-standalone-images)

For Standalone Images

1.  Navigate to Image Generation in Manus ![nano banana image.png](https://mintcdn.com/docs-manus/SsKP6I-rYVXzKghN/images/nanobananaimage.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=SsKP6I-rYVXzKghN&q=85&s=599429373bc650c7bcd3fb2b07f55369)
2.  Select “Nano Banana Pro” as your model

![Screenshot 2025-12-08 at 11.54.32 AM.png](https://mintcdn.com/docs-manus/SsKP6I-rYVXzKghN/images/Screenshot2025-12-08at11.54.32AM.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=SsKP6I-rYVXzKghN&q=85&s=b3472259cd00f8561f4011d654e7c72b)

1.  Describe the image you need with specific details
2.  Generate and download your custom visual

Example:

Copy

Ask AI

    Create a minimalist slide deck about sustainable fashion for a startup pitch.
    Use earth tones and modern typography. Include sections on market opportunity,
    our solution, and impact metrics.
    

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/integrations/nano-banana-pro#how-manus-generates-your-content)

How Manus Generates Your Content

For slide decks, Manus:

1.  Analyzes your prompt and understands your message
2.  Creates a complete presentation outline
3.  Determines visual direction (colors, layout, imagery)
4.  Batch-generates all slides with consistent design
5.  Delivers a ready-to-use deck

For standalone images, Manus generates custom visuals in moments.

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/integrations/nano-banana-pro#4-export-and-use)

4\. Export and Use

Download your slides as PDF or individual images, ready for any platform.

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/integrations/nano-banana-pro#use-dynamic-prompts)

Use Dynamic Prompts

Combine Nano Banana Pro with other Manus features for powerful, data-driven presentations: **Wide Research + Slides:**

Copy

Ask AI

    Analyze 50 SaaS pricing pages, identify patterns, then create a pricing strategy presentation in a professional B2B style with data visualizations.
    

**Data Analysis + Slides:**

Copy

Ask AI

    Analyze this sales data CSV, identify trends and insights, then create a quarterly business review deck using corporate colors and clean charts.
    

**Manus Browser Operator + Slides:**

Copy

Ask AI

    Visit these 5 competitor websites, extract their key features and pricing, then create a competitive analysis deck using a modern, minimalist design.
    

**Scheduled Tasks + Slides:**

Copy

Ask AI

    Every Monday at 9 AM: Research last week's AI news, summarize key developments, then create a weekly briefing deck using tech-forward design.
    

These combined workflows create presentations that are both visually stunning and backed by real data.

[​](https://manus.im/docs/integrations/nano-banana-pro#tips-for-effective-use)

Tips for Effective Use
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Be Specific About Style**  
✅ Good: “Minimalist design with earth tones and sans-serif typography”❌ Vague: “Make it look good”

**Include Context**✅ Good: “Pitch deck for sustainable fashion startup targeting Gen Z consumers”❌ Vague: “Fashion presentation”

**Describe Visual Elements**✅ Good: “Use photography of real products, natural lighting, lifestyle imagery”❌ Vague: “Add some pictures”

Do I need design skills to use Nano Banana Pro?

Click the 🍌 Nano Banana Pro button in the Slides interface before entering your prompt. You’ll see it next to the Slides button in the input area.

Can Manus combine research with Nano Banana Pro slides?

Yes. Manus can research topics, analyze data, or scrape websites, then automatically create visually stunning presentations with that information. Just describe the full workflow in your prompt.

Can I edit slides after Manus generates them?

Not yet, Nano Banana Pro slides are complete images with text rendered directly into the visual. For editable presentations, use Manus’s standard HTML slides instead. But Manus will support this soon. 

When should I use Nano Banana Pro vs. standard HTML slides in Manus?

Use Nano Banana Pro for high-impact visual presentations (pitches, launches, keynotes). Use HTML slides for data-heavy content you’ll update frequently or need to edit.

Does using Nano Banana Pro consume more credits?

Image generation uses credits based on complexity and quantity. Check your Manus plan details for specific credit costs per slide or image.

Next steps: Try your first [Nano Banana Pro presentation](https://manus.im/tools/nano-banana-pro-slides)
. Open Manus Slides, select a Nano Banana template, and describe your vision.

[Manus API](https://manus.im/docs/integrations/manus-api)

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/design-view#what-is-design-view)

What is Design View?
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Design View is an integrated feature that allows for complex, multi-step visual workflows. Instead of starting from scratch with every new prompt, you can make precise edits to existing images, ensuring consistency and saving valuable time. Whether you’re designing a poster, creating a mood board, or refining a product shot, Design View acts as your creative partner, understanding your intent from start to finish. It is powered by Google’s advanced Nano Banana Pro image generation model, ensuring high-quality, photorealistic results.

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/design-view#how-to-use-design-view)

How to Use Design View
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Using Design View is an intuitive process that combines simple prompts with powerful editing tools. Here’s how you can get started:

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/design-view#step-1:-generate-your-initial-concept)

Step 1: Generate Your Initial Concept

![Screenshot 2025 12 22 At 2 43 09 PM](https://mintcdn.com/docs-manus/SUBATJz3NZyTujdA/images/Screenshot2025-12-22at2.43.09PM.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=SUBATJz3NZyTujdA&q=85&s=189f62bd33bca7a49b88de648e24e721) Begin by giving Manus a simple prompt to generate your base image.

Copy

Ask AI

    A photorealistic interior shot of a bright, airy living room in a Japandi style. The room has light oak wood floors, a large window with soft natural light, and a low-profile beige sofa.
    

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/design-view#step-2:-refine-with-the-mark-tool)

Step 2: Refine with the Mark Tool

Once you have your initial image, you can use the **Mark Tool** to make precise edits. Instead of writing a new prompt and hoping for the best, you can select specific elements and provide instructions for how to change them.

1.  Click the **\[Mark\]** tool in the Design View interface. 2. Select the element you want to modify (e.g., a sofa, a plant, a window). 3. Provide a clear and concise instruction for the change.

For example: ![Screenshot 2025 12 22 At 4 40 40 PM](https://mintcdn.com/docs-manus/SUBATJz3NZyTujdA/images/Screenshot2025-12-22at4.40.40PM.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=SUBATJz3NZyTujdA&q=85&s=813fa455ea1480fd0215a7637170f7e1) \* Select the sofa: `Change this to a muted sage green.` \* Select the plant: `Change this to a wildflower arrangement.` \* Select the window: `Change the leaves to autumn foliage.`

2.  Reference Images: You can add elements to your design by providing a reference image. For example, you can add a specific lamp to a room by uploading an image of it.

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/design-view#step-3:-edit-text-elements)

Step 3: Edit Text Elements

![Screenshot 2025 12 23 At 3 04 46 PM](https://mintcdn.com/docs-manus/SUBATJz3NZyTujdA/images/Screenshot2025-12-23at3.04.46PM.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=SUBATJz3NZyTujdA&q=85&s=2373157fe62979b6128556df518309a4) If your design includes text, such as on a poster or in an infographic, you can easily edit it without disturbing the rest of the image. Click on **“edit text”** and Manus will extract all text elements, allowing you to make changes with ease.

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/design-view#mobile-editing)

Mobile Editing

Design View is also available on the Manus mobile app, so you can continue your work on the go. ![Screenshot 2025 12 23 At 3 05 27 PM](https://mintcdn.com/docs-manus/SUBATJz3NZyTujdA/images/Screenshot2025-12-23at3.05.27PM.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=SUBATJz3NZyTujdA&q=85&s=e354def500f42dce114462f356b60b03) **Press and Hold to Mark**: Simply press and hold on any area of an image to create a selection. **Voice or Text Input**: Once an area is marked, you can either type your changes or use your voice to record instructions.  
**Batch Your Edits**: Mark multiple areas on an image, add an instruction for each, and send them all to be processed in a single batch.

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/design-view#what-you-need-to-know)

What You Need to Know
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Integrated Workflow**: Design View is not a standalone tool; it is an integrated capability of the Manus agent. This allows for a seamless transition between generating ideas, refining visuals, and incorporating them into larger projects. **Precision and Control**: The Mark Tool gives you a level of control that is not possible with traditional prompting. You can change specific elements of an image without affecting the overall composition, lighting, or style.

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/design-view#tips-for-better-results)

Tips for Better Results
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Tip | Description |
| --- | --- |
| **Be Specific with Instructions** | When using the Mark Tool, provide clear and direct instructions. For example, instead of saying “make this better,” say “change the color to a deep blue.” |
| **Use High-Quality Reference Images** | When adding elements from a reference image, use a high-quality image with a clear subject for the best results. |
| **Start with a Good Base Image** | The better your initial image, the easier it will be to refine. Spend some time crafting a good initial prompt to get a strong starting point. |
| **Iterate and Refine** | Don’t be afraid to make multiple small changes to get your image just right. The power of Design View is in its iterative workflow. |

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/design-view#common-questions)

Common Questions
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

What AI model powers Manus Design View?

Design View is powered by Google’s Nano Banana Pro, a cutting-edge image generation model

How is this different from other AI image generators?

Design View is not a standalone tool; it is an integrated capability of the Manus agent that allows for complex, multi-step visual workflows. The key difference is the ability to make precise, in-context edits to existing images, rather than regenerating a new image from scratch with every prompt.

Is Design View available on all Manus plans?

Yes, Manus Design View is available to all Manus users.

[Wide Research](https://manus.im/docs/features/wide-research)

⌘I

[​](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/getting-started#intro:-the-all-in-one-workflow)

Intro: The All-in-One Workflow
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Manus transforms web development from a fragmented, multi-tool process into a single, seamless, and conversational workflow. It is not just a website builder; it is a comprehensive platform that handles everything from initial research and content creation to deployment and post-launch analytics. With Manus, you can execute the entire value chain of web development within one unified environment.

This all-in-one approach means you can:

*   **Research and Strategize**: Use Manus to research your target audience, analyze competitors, and formulate a content strategy.
*   **Create Content and Assets**: Generate high-quality text and images for your website using built-in AI capabilities.
*   **Build and Develop**: Construct full-stack applications with backends, databases, and user authentication through simple, natural language commands.
*   **Integrate and Extend**: Connect to external services like [Stripe](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/payments)
     for payments or Google Maps for location-based features.
*   **Deploy and Host**: Publish your application to the web with a single command, with all hosting and infrastructure managed by Manus.
*   **Analyze and Iterate**: Track user behavior with built-in analytics and use those insights to continuously improve your application.

This integrated workflow eliminates the need to juggle multiple tools, manage complex configurations, or write a single line of code. By consolidating the entire process, Manus empowers you to build and launch sophisticated web applications faster and more efficiently than ever before.

[​](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/getting-started#getting-started:-your-first-app-in-minutes)

Getting Started: Your First App in Minutes
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Building a web application with Manus is designed to be a fast and intuitive process. This guide provides the essential steps to get your first project up and running.

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/getting-started#1-initiate-your-project)

1\. Initiate Your Project

Start by telling Manus what you want to build in plain English. The more descriptive you are, the better the initial result will be. For example:

> “Build me a modern landing page for a new SaaS product. It should have a hero section with a signup button, a features section, a pricing table, and a footer.”

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/getting-started#2-review-and-refine-the-plan)

2\. Review and Refine the Plan

Mantus will analyze your request and present a development plan. This plan outlines the structure, features, and technologies it intends to use. At this stage, you can provide feedback or ask for adjustments before the build process begins.

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/getting-started#3-watch-manus-build)

3\. Watch Manus Build

Once you approve the plan, Manus gets to work. You can watch in real-time as it scaffolds the project, writes the code for both the frontend and backend, and configures all the necessary components. A live, interactive preview of your application is available from the very beginning.

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/getting-started#4-iterate-with-natural-language)

4\. Iterate with Natural Language

With the live preview, you can instantly see the results of your requests. If you want to make changes, you don’t need to write code. Simply describe what you want to modify:

> “Change the color of the signup button to a vibrant blue.”

Or, for more structural changes:

> “Add a testimonial section between the features and pricing sections.”

Manus will understand your instructions and update the application instantly. This conversational approach makes iteration incredibly fast and allows you to focus on the creative aspects of your project.  
  
Check out some web applications we built [here](https://manusai.notion.site/Manus-Web-App-Use-Cases-2927ff657cfa8174a2a1fedb6bece124)

[Editing and Previewing](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/editing-and-previewing)

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/wide-research#what-is-wide-research)

What is Wide Research?
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Wide Research is Manus’s approach to handling tasks that involve processing many similar items—such as analyzing 100 products, researching 50 companies, or generating 20 pieces of content. Instead of using a single AI agent that processes items sequentially, Wide Research deploys hundreds of independent agents that work in parallel. Each agent receives its own dedicated context and processes one item independently. This architecture solves the context window limitation that causes traditional AI systems to degrade in quality as the number of items increases.

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/wide-research#the-context-window-problem)

The Context Window Problem
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Traditional AI systems, including most chatbots, operate with a fixed context window—a limit on how much information they can actively process at once. When asked to analyze many items sequentially:

*   **Items 1-5**: Detailed, thorough analysis with full context available
*   **Items 10-20**: Descriptions become shorter as context fills up
*   **Items 30+**: Generic summaries and increased errors as earlier context is compressed or lost

This degradation occurs because the AI must keep all previous items in memory while processing new ones. Research shows this “fabrication threshold” typically occurs around 8-10 items for most AI systems.

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/wide-research#how-wide-research-works)

How Wide Research Works
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Wide Research uses a fundamentally different architecture: **1\. Task Decomposition**: The main agent analyzes your request and breaks it into independent sub-tasks (e.g., “research company #1”, “research company #2”, etc.) **2\. Parallel Agent Deployment**: Each sub-task is assigned to a dedicated agent with its own fresh context window **3\. Independent Processing**: Agents work simultaneously, each conducting thorough research without competing for context space **4\. Result Synthesis**: The main agent collects all completed sub-tasks and assembles them into your requested format (table, report, dataset, etc.) **Result**: Item #250 receives the same depth of analysis as item #1, because each has its own dedicated agent and full context window.

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/wide-research#quick-start)

Use Cases by Category
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Category | Example Tasks |
| --- | --- |
| **Market Research** | Compare 100 products, analyze competitor pricing, survey customer reviews |
| **Academic Research** | Literature review of 50 papers, analyze research trends, compare methodologies |
| **Competitive Intelligence** | Profile 30 competitors, analyze feature sets, track pricing changes |
| **Lead Generation** | Research 200 prospects, find contact info, qualify leads |
| **Content Creation** | Generate 20 blog outlines, create 50 social posts, write 30 product descriptions |
| **Data Extraction** | Scrape 100 websites, extract structured data, compile databases |
| **Creative Production** | Generate 20 images, edit 50 photos, create consistent brand assets |
| **Investment Research** | Analyze 40 startups, compare 30 funds, research 50 portfolio companie |

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/wide-research#why-wide-research-vs-other-tools)

Why Wide Research vs. Other Tools
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Aspect | AI Chatbot | Manus Wide Research |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **Approach** | Single AI helps you | Parallel multi-agent orchestration |
| **Speed** | Hours until context saturation | Minutes regardless of scale |
| **Scale** | Degrades beyond 8-10 items | Scales to hundreds seamlessly |
| **Quality** | Progressive degradation | Uniform quality at any scale |
| **Output** | Compressed summaries with detail loss | Complete reports and datasets |

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/wide-research#when-to-use-wide-research)

When to Use Wide Research
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Perfect For**:

*   Competitive intelligence (analyze 50+ competitors)
*   Market research (compare 100+ products)
*   Academic research (review 30+ papers)
*   Lead generation (research 200+ prospects)
*   Content creation (generate 20+ similar items)
*   Data extraction (scrape and structure 100+ pages)
*   Batch processing (edit 50+ images/files)

**Not Ideal For**:

*   Single deep-dive analysis (use regular agent mode)
*   Tasks requiring sequential dependencies
*   Real-time interactive research
*   Tasks with fewer than 10 items

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/wide-research#tips-for-better-results)

Tips for Better Results
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Be specific about structure**:

*   ✅ “Create a table with columns: name, company, role, email, LinkedIn”
*   ❌ “Research these people”

**Specify the scale upfront**:

*   ✅ “Analyze all 100 companies in this list”
*   ❌ “Analyze some companies”

**Describe desired output format**:

*   ✅ “Organize in a sortable spreadsheet with filters”
*   ❌ “Give me the results”

**Include evaluation criteria**:

*   ✅ “Rate each product on: price, features, reviews, availability”
*   ❌ “Compare these products”

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/wide-research#common-questions)

Common Questions
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

How many items can Wide Research handle?

Tested up to 250 items. Theoretically unlimited, but practical limit depends on task complexity.

How long does it take?

Depends on task complexity and scale. Typically minutes for 50-100 items, regardless of depth.

Can I refine results after?

Yes. Ask for modifications: “Add a column for pricing” or “Re-research items 20-30 with more detail.”

Does it work for non-research tasks?

 Yes. Any task that involves processing multiple independent items: image editing, data extraction, content generation, etc.

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/wide-research#)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Export Formats
---------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   PowerPoint (.pptx): Fully editable in PowerPoint or Google Slides
*   PDF: Print-ready for distribution
*   Web Slides: Interactive browser-based presentation
*   Speaker Notes Document: Separate file with all notes

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/slides#tips-for-better-presentations)

Tips for Better Presentations
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Be specific about audience:

*   ✅ “Technical audience familiar with ML”
*   ✅ “Business executives, no technical background”
*   ❌ “General audience”

Define the goal:

*   ✅ “Convince investors to fund us”
*   ✅ “Educate students on the basics”
*   ❌ “Present information”

Specify length and timing:

*   ✅ “15 slides for 20-minute presentation”
*   ✅ “30 slides for 1-hour workshop”
*   ❌ “Make some slides”

Let Manus research:

*   ✅ “Research current market trends and include them”
*   ❌ Providing all content yourself

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/slides#common-questions)

Common Questions
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Can I edit slides after creation? Yes. Download the .pptx file and edit in any presentation software.** How long does it take? 5-15 minutes depending on complexity. Simple 10-slide deck: ~5 min. Complex 40-slide research presentation: ~15 min. **Can Manus use my company template? Yes. Upload your .pptx template file.** What if I need changes? Ask Manus to make changes through conversation, or edit the PowerPoint file directly. **Can Manus create charts from my data? Yes. Upload your data (CSV, Excel), and Manus will create appropriate visualizations.** What languages are supported? All major languages. Specify in your request: “Create in Spanish…”

[Introduction](https://manus.im/docs/introduction/welcome)

Manus-built web applications are not just static sites; they are intelligent, dynamic platforms with AI capabilities woven into their core. This allows you to create unique and engaging experiences for your users.

[​](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/ai-capabilities#large-language-model-llm)

Large Language Model (LLM)
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can integrate the power of large language models directly into your application to create features that understand and generate human-like text. This opens up a world of possibilities for interactivity and user assistance.

| Use Case | Example Prompt |
| --- | --- |
| **AI-Powered Chatbot** | `"Add a chatbot to the bottom right corner of the site. It should be able to answer frequently asked questions about our pricing, features, and return policy."` |
| **Content Generation Tool** | `"Create a new page called 'Blog Post Helper'. Add a text input field and a button. When the user enters a topic and clicks the button, call the LLM to generate a 100-word blog post introduction on that topic and display it below."` |
| **Natural Language Search** | `"Upgrade the search bar in the header to use natural language processing. When a user searches for 'cheap red shoes for running', it should understand the intent and show relevant products from the database."` |
| **Automated Summarization** | `"On the article pages, add a 'Summarize' button. When clicked, use the LLM to generate a three-bullet-point summary of the article's content."` |

[​](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/ai-capabilities#image-generation)

Image Generation
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In addition to text-based AI, you can also incorporate dynamic image generation into your application. This enables a wide range of creative and personalized visual experiences.

| Use Case | Example Prompt |
| --- | --- |
| **Personalized Avatars** | `"On the user profile page, add a feature to generate a personalized avatar. The user can enter a text description like 'a friendly robot with a blue hat', and the app should generate and display the image."` |
| **Dynamic Product Mockups** | `"On the product page for our custom t-shirts, add a section where users can input text. Use the image generation model to create a mockup of the t-shirt with their custom text printed on it."` |
| **Creative Backgrounds** | `"Create a 'background generator' tool. Add a text area where users can describe a scene, like 'a futuristic cityscape at sunset, in a watercolor style'. Generate a high-resolution background image based on their description."` |
| **AI-Generated Illustrations** | `"For our blog, create a feature that generates a unique header image for each new post based on the post's title and a summary of its content."` |

# Publishing - Manus Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/publishing#content-area)

[Manus Documentation home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/docs-manus/C1PisAhqAuyVufRp/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=C1PisAhqAuyVufRp&q=85&s=7366a98aefb64c7c37c7dd35d613c640)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/docs-manus/C1PisAhqAuyVufRp/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=C1PisAhqAuyVufRp&q=85&s=1b58c59477c90d5dbf1454f25864b789)](https://manus.im/docs)

Getting Started

Publishing

[Introduction](https://manus.im/docs/introduction/welcome)
[Features](https://manus.im/docs/features/design-view)
[Website Builder](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/getting-started)
[Integrations](https://manus.im/docs/integrations/integrations)

On this page

*   [The Publishing Process](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/publishing#the-publishing-process)
    
*   [Custom Domains: Professionalize Your Brand](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/publishing#custom-domains%3A-professionalize-your-brand)
    
*   [Connecting Your Domain](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/publishing#connecting-your-domain)
    
*   [Purchasing a Domain](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/publishing#purchasing-a-domain)
    
*   [Automatic SSL/HTTPS](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/publishing#automatic-ssl%2Fhttps)
    

With Manus, publishing your web application is a straightforward, one-step process. There are no servers to configure, no deployment pipelines to build, and no complex technical hurdles to overcome.

[​](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/publishing#the-publishing-process)

The Publishing Process
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **Finalize Your Application**: Ensure that you have completed all the necessary edits and tested your application in the preview window.
2.  **Give the Command**: Tell Manus to publish your application. For example:
    
    > “Publish this website and make it live.”
    
3.  **Manus Handles the Rest**: Manus will take care of the entire deployment process, including:
    *   Provisioning the necessary cloud infrastructure.
    *   Building and optimizing your application for production.
    *   Deploying it to a secure, scalable hosting environment.
    *   Configuring the necessary DNS settings if you are using a custom domain.

Your application will be live and accessible to your users within minutes. You can continue to make changes and update your application at any time by simply describing the modifications you want, and Manus will handle the redeployment process automatically.

[​](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/publishing#custom-domains:-professionalize-your-brand)

Custom Domains: Professionalize Your Brand
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Give your web application a professional and memorable address by connecting your own custom domain. Manus makes it easy to publish your site to any domain or subdomain that you own.

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/publishing#connecting-your-domain)

Connecting Your Domain

To connect your domain, you simply need to tell Manus which domain you want to use. For example:

> “Publish this site to my custom domain, [www.example.com](http://www.example.com/)
> .”

Manus will then provide you with the necessary DNS records that you will need to add to your domain registrar’s settings. This typically involves adding or updating an A record or a CNAME record.

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/publishing#purchasing-a-domain)

Purchasing a Domain

Purchasing a custom domain inside Manus is now one of the fastest steps in going live. Instead of bouncing between external registrars and juggling DNS settings, you can search, buy, and secure your domain directly within the builder. Everything updates on the same page, and Manus handles the setup behind the scenes. This means you can move from prototype to a fully branded, public site in minutes. Whether you are launching your first product or taking an existing project live, buying your domain through Manus keeps the entire process simple, consistent, and fast.

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/publishing#automatic-ssl/https)

Automatic SSL/HTTPS

Security is handled automatically. Once your domain is connected, Manus will provision and configure a free SSL/TLS certificate for your site. This ensures that all traffic to and from your application is encrypted, providing a secure experience for your users and improving your site’s search engine ranking.

[Editing and Previewing](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/editing-and-previewing)

# Editing and Previewing - Manus Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/editing-and-previewing#content-area)

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/editing-and-previewing#edit:-effortless,-conversational-changes)

Edit: Effortless, Conversational Changes

Editing your web application in Manus is as simple as having a conversation. There is no need to write code or navigate complex menus. You can make changes to your site by describing what you want in natural language, from single tweaks to large-scale updates.

#### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/editing-and-previewing#visual-editing)

Visual Editing

Manus 1.5 introduced 3 flexible ways to edit your websites:

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/editing-and-previewing#quick-style-controls)

**Quick Style Controls**

Click any element to open an instant style panel. No waiting, no prompts—just direct control:

*   Colors: Change backgrounds, text, borders
*   Typography: Adjust fonts, sizes, weights
*   Spacing: Modify padding, margins, gaps
*   Borders: Update styles, widths, radius

Perfect for rapid design iteration and fine-tuning.

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/editing-and-previewing#prompt-based-batch-editing)

**Prompt-Based Batch Editing**

To make your workflow even more efficient, Manus allows you to perform **prompt-based group edits**. You can describe multiple changes in a single prompt, and Manus will intelligently package and apply them together as a single update. This is perfect for making a series of related adjustments without having to issue commands one by one. For example, you can give a single, comprehensive instruction like this:

> “Okay, let’s make a few changes. First, make the main heading bolder and change its color to our brand’s dark blue. Next, adjust the spacing in the pricing table to be more generous. Finally, change the background color of the entire footer section to a light gray.”

Manus will understand the distinct requests within your prompt and execute all of them in one go, saving you time and effort.

| Edit Type | Example Prompt |
| --- | --- |
| **Styling** | `"Change the font of all headings to Georgia."` |
| **Layout** | `"Increase the spacing between the items in this list."` |
| **Content** | `"Change the text of the main button to 'Get Started Now'."` |
| **Structure** | `"Duplicate this section and place it below the contact form."` |

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/editing-and-previewing#ai-edit:-your-creative-partner)

AI Edit: Your Creative Partner

For more complex or creative changes, you can use the AI edit feature. Simply select an element and ask Manus to improve it. This is like having a design consultant and copywriter at your fingertips.

| Goal | Example Prompt |
| --- | --- |
| **Improve Copy** | `"Rewrite this headline to be more engaging and benefit-oriented."` |
| **Enhance Design** | `"Suggest a better, more modern color palette for this section."` |
| **Refine Layout** | `"Restructure this feature list to be more visually appealing and easier to scan."` |

Manus will provide suggestions and apply the changes for you, making it easy to elevate your design and content beyond the quality of your content. Manus provides a seamless experience for editing and previewing your web application in real-time. This allows for rapid iteration and ensures that you can visualize changes as you make them.

[​](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/editing-and-previewing#preview:-see-your-application-in-real-time)

Preview: See Your Application in Real-Time
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Manus provides a live, interactive preview of your web application throughout the entire development process. This allows you to see your changes as they happen and test your application’s functionality in a real-world environment.

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/editing-and-previewing#desktop/mobile)

Desktop/Mobile

The preview window allows you to toggle between desktop and mobile views, ensuring your application is responsive and looks great on all devices. You can test the user experience on different screen sizes and make adjustments as needed to optimize for both desktop and mobile users.

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/editing-and-previewing#path)

Path

The preview window includes a URL bar that displays the current path of the page you are viewing. This is useful for navigating to specific pages within your application and for understanding the URL structure of your site.

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/editing-and-previewing#fullscreen)

Fullscreen

For a more immersive experience, you can expand the preview to fullscreen mode. This is particularly useful for presenting your application to stakeholders or for getting a better sense of the overall look and feel of your site without the distraction of the surrounding interface.

#### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/editing-and-previewing#live-preview)

Live Preview

A live, interactive preview of your application is available from the very beginning of the development process. This allows you to see the results of your requests instantly and provide feedback for adjustments. The live preview is an essential part of the iterative development process, enabling you to refine your application with natural language commands and see the changes reflected immediately.

[Getting started](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/getting-started)
[Publishing](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/publishing)

# Scheduled Tasks - Manus Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://manus.im/docs/features/scheduled-tasks#content-area)

Scheduled Tasks

Scheduled Tasks let you automate recurring work by having Manus execute tasks on a schedule. Set it once, and Manus handles it automatically—daily reports, weekly research, monthly analysis, or any recurring workflow.

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/scheduled-tasks#quick-start)

Quick Start
------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/scheduled-tasks#one-time-task)

One-Time Task

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/scheduled-tasks#recurring-task)

Recurring Task

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/scheduled-tasks#complex-schedule)

Complex Schedule

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/scheduled-tasks#when-to-use-scheduled-tasks)

When to Use Scheduled Tasks
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Use for:

*   **Recurring research** (daily news summaries, weekly competitor updates)
*   **Regular reports** (monthly analytics, weekly performance summaries)
*   **Periodic data collection** (scraping prices, tracking mentions)
*   **Automated monitoring** (checking for updates, tracking changes)

Don’t use for:

*   One-off tasks you need right now (just run them normally)
*   Real-time monitoring (scheduled tasks run at specific times, not continuously)

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/scheduled-tasks#quick-examples)

Quick Examples
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/scheduled-tasks#example-1:-daily-news-digest)

Example 1: Daily News Digest

**Schedule**: Daily at 7 AM (weekdays only) **Output**: Email with curated news summary

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/scheduled-tasks#example-2:-weekly-competitor-tracking)

Example 2: Weekly Competitor Tracking

**Schedule**: Weekly (Fridays at 5 PM) **Output**: Comparison table in Google Drive

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/scheduled-tasks#example-3:-monthly-analytics-report)

Example 3: Monthly Analytics Report

**Schedule**: Monthly (1st day at 9 AM) **Output**: Slide deck posted to Slack

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/scheduled-tasks#how-to-set-up)

How to Set Up
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Step 1: Describe the task** Be specific about what you want Manus to do. **Step 2: Specify the schedule**

*   “Every day at 9 AM”
*   “Every Monday at 8 AM”
*   “On the 1st of every month”
*   “Every weekday at 7 AM”
*   “Tomorrow at 3 PM” (one-time)

**Step 3: Define the output**

*   Email results to you
*   Post to Slack channel
*   Save to Google Drive
*   Update a spreadsheet
*   Send via connector

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/scheduled-tasks#schedule-options)

Schedule Options
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Schedule Type | Example | Use Case |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **Daily** | ”Every day at 9 AM” | News summaries, daily metrics |
| **Weekdays** | ”Every weekday at 8 AM” | Business reports, work updates |
| **Weekly** | ”Every Monday at 10 AM” | Weekly reviews, competitor tracking |
| **Monthly** | ”On the 1st at 9 AM” | Monthly reports, billing analysis |
| **Custom** | ”Every Tuesday and Thursday at 2 PM” | Specific recurring needs |
| **One-Time** | ”Tomorrow at 3 PM” | Delayed execution |

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/scheduled-tasks#managing-scheduled-tasks)

Managing Scheduled Tasks
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**View active schedules**: Navigate to Settings → Scheduled Tasks to see all active schedules. **Pause a schedule**: Toggle off any schedule temporarily without deleting it. **Edit a schedule**: Modify timing, task description, or output method. **Delete a schedule**: Remove schedules you no longer need. **View execution history**: See past runs, results, and any errors.

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/scheduled-tasks#tips-for-better-scheduled-tasks)

Tips for Better Scheduled Tasks
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Be specific about timing**:

*   ✅ “Every weekday at 8 AM EST”
*   ❌ “In the morning”

**Define clear outputs**:

*   ✅ “Email me a 5-bullet summary”
*   ✅ “Post to Slack #team channel”
*   ❌ “Let me know what you find”

**Include time ranges for research**:

*   ✅ “News from the past 24 hours”
*   ✅ “Updates since last week”
*   ❌ “Recent news” (ambiguous)

**Test before scheduling**:

*   Run the task manually first to ensure it works as expected
*   Then set up the schedule

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/scheduled-tasks#quick-use-cases)

Quick Use Cases
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Use Case | Schedule | Output |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **News Monitoring** | Daily 7 AM | Email summary |
| **Competitor Tracking** | Weekly Friday 5 PM | Google Drive report |
| **Social Media Monitoring** | Daily 9 AM | Slack notification |
| **Analytics Reports** | Monthly 1st day | Slide deck |
| **Price Tracking** | Daily 6 AM | Spreadsheet update |
| **Content Curation** | Weekdays 8 AM | Email digest |

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/scheduled-tasks#common-questions)

Common Questions
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

What happens if a scheduled task fails?

Manus will notify you and log the error. You can review the issue and adjust the task.

Can I run a task immediately and also schedule it?

Yes. Run it now to test, then set up the recurring schedule.

What timezone are schedules in

Your account timezone (set in Settings). You can specify timezone in the schedule: “9 AM EST”

How many scheduled tasks can I have?

Depends on your plan. Check Settings → Scheduled Tasks for your limit.

Can I schedule Wide Research tasks?

Yes. Any task Manus can do can be scheduled.

* * *

[Data Analysis & Visualization](https://manus.im/docs/features/data-visualization)

# Manus Collab - Manus Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://manus.im/docs/features/collab#content-area)

[Manus Documentation home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/docs-manus/C1PisAhqAuyVufRp/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=C1PisAhqAuyVufRp&q=85&s=7366a98aefb64c7c37c7dd35d613c640)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/docs-manus/C1PisAhqAuyVufRp/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=C1PisAhqAuyVufRp&q=85&s=1b58c59477c90d5dbf1454f25864b789)](https://manus.im/docs)

![US](https://d3gk2c5xim1je2.cloudfront.net/flags/US.svg)

Manus Collab

[Introduction](https://manus.im/docs/introduction/welcome)
[Features](https://manus.im/docs/features/design-view)

On this page

*   [How It Works](https://manus.im/docs/features/collab#how-it-works)
    
*   [Enabling Collaboration](https://manus.im/docs/features/collab#enabling-collaboration)

*   [Tips for Effective Collaboration](https://manus.im/docs/features/collab#tips-for-effective-collaboration)
    
*   [Common Questions](https://manus.im/docs/features/collab#common-questions)
    

Manus Collab is a real-time collaboration feature that enables teams to work together on Manus tasks. Instead of juggling multiple document versions, scattered email feedback, and endless “latest\_final\_v3” files, Collab provides one shared workspace where your entire team can prompt, edit, and refine work simultaneously. When you enable collaboration on a task, you create a single source of truth accessible via one link. Everyone sees updates instantly, everyone can interact with Manus directly, and only the task owner consumes credits.

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/collab#how-it-works)

How It Works
-----------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/collab#enabling-collaboration)

Enabling Collaboration

**Step 1**: Open the task that needs collaboration **Step 2**: Find the share button in the task interface ![collaborate](https://mintcdn.com/docs-manus/C1PisAhqAuyVufRp/images/collaborate.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=C1PisAhqAuyVufRp&q=85&s=54d501a1a60c65350e8d89fd2ef5a34b) **Step 3**: Click and select “Collaboration” (not just “Share”) **Step 4**: Enter email addresses of collaborators ![Screenshot2025 11 24at11 51 30AM Pn](https://mintcdn.com/docs-manus/qyTF8fL1fXZWZJSU/images/Screenshot2025-11-24at11.51.30AM.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=qyTF8fL1fXZWZJSU&q=85&s=75f64fc85475ad517337c9dcd80774ba) **Step 5**: Collaborators receive invitation and can join immediately

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/collab#real-time-collaboration)

Real-Time Collaboration

Once enabled, all participants can:

*   **View the task** in real-time as it develops
*   **Prompt Manus directly** to make changes or additions ![Screenshot2025 11 24at11 49 42AM Pn](https://mintcdn.com/docs-manus/qyTF8fL1fXZWZJSU/images/Screenshot2025-11-24at11.49.42AM.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=qyTF8fL1fXZWZJSU&q=85&s=6f754c315a5becdb9133a37436de22c8)
*   **See everyone’s prompts** and Manus’s responses instantly
*   **Iterate together** without waiting for exports or updates

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/collab#example-workflow)

Example Workflow

**Creating a quarterly review presentation**

1

Task owner

Create a Q4 performance review deck with sales data, key wins, and goals for Q1_Manus generates initial deck_

2

Marketing lead

Add a slide about our social media growth—we hit 50K followers_Manus adds the slide_

3

Sales lead

![Screenshot2025 11 24at11 49 56AM Pn](https://mintcdn.com/docs-manus/qyTF8fL1fXZWZJSU/images/Screenshot2025-11-24at11.49.56AM.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=qyTF8fL1fXZWZJSU&q=85&s=d7b5f0a2177a5d7e6fa1f217f526faf0)Increase font size on the revenue chart—hard to read_Manus updates the chart_

4

Task owner

Add speaker notes for each slide_Manus generates speaker notes_

**Result**: Complete, polished presentation created collaboratively in one session, no version conflicts.

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/collab#key-features)

Key Features
-----------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/collab#only-owner-consumes-credits)

Only Owner Consumes Credits

**Important**: In collaboration mode, only the task owner’s credits are consumed. Collaborators can participate fully without using their own credits. This makes Collab ideal for:

*   Teams with mixed subscription levels
*   Collaborating with clients or external partners
*   Onboarding new team members
*   Cross-functional projects

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/collab#owner-controlled-invitations)

Owner-Controlled Invitations

Only the task owner can invite collaborators. Collaborators cannot invite additional people. This maintains control over:

*   Who has access to the task
*   Sensitive information visibility
*   Credit consumption responsibility

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/collab#benefits)

Benefits
---------------------------------------------------------------

| Benefit | Description |
| --- | --- |
| **Zero Version Confusion** | One workspace, always current—no “final\_v3” files |
| **Real-Time Updates** | See changes instantly as team members prompt Manus |
| **Direct AI Interaction** | Everyone can prompt Manus, not just the owner |
| **Cost Efficient** | Only owner consumes credits, collaborators free |
| **Faster Iteration** | No export-feedback-revise cycles |
| **Single Source of Truth** | One link, one version, one workspace |
| **Transparent Process** | See all prompts and changes in real-time |

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/collab#important-notes)

Important Notes
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/collab#privacy-and-content-sharing)

Privacy and Content Sharing

*   **Do not share personal information** without permission during collaboration
*   **Do not share third-party content** without proper authorization
*   **Comply with Terms of Use**: All participants must follow Manus platform policies

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/collab#sandbox-login-cookies)

Sandbox Login Cookies

**Important**: When the first collaborator joins a task, the sandbox environment login cookies are cleared. **What this means**:

*   If the task involves authenticated websites (e.g., logged into a CRM), you’ll need to log in again
*   This is a security measure to protect your credentials
*   Only affects tasks using Browser Operator or Cloud Browser with logins

**Workaround**: Complete authenticated portions of the task before inviting collaborators, or be prepared to re-authenticate.

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/collab#when-to-use-collab)

When to Use Collab
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Ideal For**:

*   Team content creation (presentations, reports, articles)
*   Client co-creation and feedback
*   Cross-functional projects requiring multiple perspectives
*   Iterative design and refinement
*   Training and onboarding (show how Manus works)
*   Research projects with multiple contributors

**Not Ideal For**:

*   Solo tasks that don’t require input
*   Highly sensitive work requiring strict access control
*   Tasks where version history tracking is critical
*   Simple, quick requests

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/collab#tips-for-effective-collaboration)

Tips for Effective Collaboration
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Set clear roles**:

*   Designate who handles which aspects (content, design, data)
*   Owner should guide overall direction
*   Collaborators focus on specific contributions

**Use specific prompts**:

*   ✅ “Add a slide about Q4 sales performance with the numbers from the spreadsheet”
*   ❌ “Make it better”

**Communicate in the task**:

*   Use prompts to explain changes: “Adding customer testimonials because…”
*   This creates a clear record of decisions

**Invite strategically**:

*   Start with core team members
*   Add others as needed
*   Remember: owner controls invitations

**Be mindful of timing**:

*   Coordinate major changes to avoid conflicts
*   Use async collaboration for different time zones
*   Real-time sessions for rapid iteration

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/collab#common-questions)

Common Questions
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Can collaborators invite others?

No. Only the task owner can invite collaborators. This maintains control over access and credit consumption.

Do collaborators need a Manus account?

Yes. Collaborators receive an invitation and need to sign in to Manus to access the task.

Can I remove a collaborator?

Yes. The task owner can manage collaborator access through the sharing settings.

Can collaborators see the entire task history?

Yes. All collaborators see the complete task history, including prompts and outputs from before they joined.

What if two people prompt Manus at the same time?

Manus processes prompts sequentially. Both will be completed, but one after the other.

Can collaborators export the results?

Yes. All collaborators can access and export the task outputs.

Does Collab work with all Manus features?

Yes. Collab works with slides, web development, research, data analysis, and all other Manus capabilities.

[Mail Manus](https://manus.im/docs/features/mail-manus)
[Cloud browser](https://manus.im/docs/features/cloud-browser)
