What is Data Analysis & Visualization?
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Manus transforms raw data files into polished visual insights without requiring spreadsheet expertise or manual chart creation. Upload your data, describe what you want to learn, and Manus handles the analysis, creates professional visualizations, and delivers results in your preferred format, slides, reports, dashboards, or webpages. Manus performs actual analysis, identifies patterns, extracts insights, and presents findings in a format ready for client meetings, executive presentations, or strategic decision-making.

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/data-visualization#quick-start)

Quick Start
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![Screenshot2025 11 24at11 55 26AM Pn](https://mintcdn.com/docs-manus/mUQ72J5nIa51waf-/images/Screenshot2025-11-24at11.55.26AM.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=mUQ72J5nIa51waf-&q=85&s=6762a004dfaec906b6d27616236471be)

1.  On the [manus.im](http://manus.im/)
     main page, click on More > Visualization
2.  **Upload Data**: Provide your data file (CSV, Excel, or other formats). This could be sales data, customer surveys, market research, financial records, or any structured dataset.
3.  **Describe Your Analysis**: Use natural language to explain what you want to understand. Examples: “Identify growth opportunities and key metrics,” “Compare performance across regions,” “Find patterns in customer behavior.”
4.  **Choose Output Format**: Select how you want results delivered—slide deck, interactive dashboard, detailed report, or standalone webpage. Manus generates professional, presentation-ready output with charts, insights, and key findings.

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/data-visualization#market-trend-analysis)

Market Trend Analysis

![Screenshot2025 11 24at12 00 52PM Pn](https://mintcdn.com/docs-manus/mUQ72J5nIa51waf-/images/Screenshot2025-11-24at12.00.52PM.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=mUQ72J5nIa51waf-&q=85&s=3d86b1b845f105a207bf11a5be4ed486) **Request**: “Analyze this sales data and identify seasonal patterns, top-performing products, and growth opportunities” **Data**: 12 months of product sales across multiple categories **Output**: Slide deck with line charts showing seasonal trends, bar charts comparing product performance, and strategic recommendations based on patterns identified

* * *

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/data-visualization#customer-segmentation)

Customer Segmentation

**Request**: “Segment these customers by behavior and create profiles for each group” **Data**: Customer purchase history, demographics, engagement metrics **Output**: Interactive dashboard with scatter plots showing customer clusters, pie charts for segment distribution, and detailed profiles for each customer type

* * *

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/data-visualization#competitive-benchmarking)

Competitive Benchmarking

**Request**: “Compare our metrics against competitors and highlight where we lead or lag” **Data**: Performance metrics from 10 companies in the industry **Output**: Report with radar charts showing multi-dimensional comparison, bar charts for individual metrics, and strategic insights about competitive positioning

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/data-visualization#visualization-options)

Visualization Options
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Manus supports a comprehensive range of chart types, allowing you to select up to five different visualization styles for a single analysis. This ensures your data is presented in the most effective format for your audience.

| Chart Type | Best For |
| --- | --- |
| **Bar Charts** | Comparing values across categories, showing rankings |
| **Line Charts** | Displaying trends over time, showing growth patterns |
| **Pie Charts** | Illustrating proportions and percentage breakdowns |
| **Scatter Plots** | Revealing correlations and relationships between variables |
| **Heat Maps** | Showing intensity patterns across two dimensions |
| **Radar Charts** | Multi-dimensional comparisons, competitive analysis |

**Mix and Match**: Select multiple chart types for comprehensive analysis. For example, combine line charts (trends), bar charts (comparisons), and pie charts (composition) in a single output.

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/data-visualization#output-formats)

Output Formats
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/data-visualization#slide-decks)

Slide Decks

**What You Get**: Complete presentation with title slide, executive summary, individual charts with insights, and conclusions. **Best For**: Client presentations, executive briefings, team meetings, investor updates. **Features**: Professional design, speaker notes, export to PowerPoint, ready to present.

* * *

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/data-visualization#interactive-dashboards)

Interactive Dashboards

**What You Get**: Web-based dashboard with multiple visualizations, filters, and interactive elements. **Best For**: Ongoing monitoring, team collaboration, self-service exploration. **Features**: Real-time updates, clickable charts, responsive design, shareable link.

* * *

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/data-visualization#detailed-reports)

Detailed Reports

**What You Get**: Comprehensive document with methodology, findings, visualizations, and recommendations. **Best For**: Strategic planning, documentation, detailed analysis, audit trails. **Features**: Professional formatting, citations, export to PDF, full context.

* * *

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/data-visualization#standalone-webpages)

Standalone Webpages

**What You Get**: Public or private webpage with visualizations and narrative. **Best For**: Sharing with external stakeholders, embedding in websites, public reporting. **Features**: Custom branding, responsive design, no login required, permanent link.

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/data-visualization#real-world-use-cases)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

###

Sales Performance Analysis

**Scenario**: Quarterly sales review for executive team**Data**: Sales transactions, customer data, product performance**Output**: Slide deck with regional comparison bar charts, product trend lines, customer segment pie charts, and strategic recommendations**Result**: Executive-ready presentation delivered in minutes instead of hours of manual Excel work

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/data-visualization#customer-survey-insights)

Customer Survey Insights

**Scenario**: Understanding customer satisfaction and pain points**Data**: Survey responses from 500 customers**Analysis**: “Analyze satisfaction scores, identify common complaints, and segment by customer type”**Output**: Report with satisfaction trend lines, complaint category bar charts, customer segment profiles, and improvement recommendations**Result**: Actionable insights with professional visualizations for product team

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/data-visualization#market-research-compilation)

Market Research Compilation

**Scenario**: Competitive landscape analysis for strategy meeting**Data**: Competitor data from Wide Research (pricing, features, market position)**Analysis**: “Create competitive positioning map and identify our differentiation opportunities”**Output**: Interactive dashboard with scatter plot positioning map, feature comparison heat map, pricing analysis bar charts**Result**: Strategic insights visualized for immediate decision-making

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/data-visualization#financial-trend-monitoring)

Financial Trend Monitoring

**Scenario**: Monthly financial review for board meeting**Data**: Revenue, expenses, cash flow over 24 months**Analysis**: “Show revenue trends, expense breakdown, and cash flow projections”**Output**: Slide deck with revenue line charts, expense pie charts, cash flow waterfall charts, and financial health summary**Result**: Board-ready financial presentation with professional visualizations

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/data-visualization#when-to-use-data-analysis-&-visualization)

When to Use Data Analysis & Visualization
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Ideal For**:

*   Preparing presentations from raw data
*   Client meetings requiring visual insights
*   Executive briefings and board reports
*   Market research synthesis
*   Performance reviews and KPI tracking
*   Customer behavior analysis
*   Competitive benchmarking
*   Financial reporting

**Not Ideal For**:

*   Real-time data streaming (use static datasets)
*   Highly specialized statistical modeling (use dedicated tools)
*   Data that requires extensive cleaning (clean first, then analyze)
*   Exploratory data science (better suited for structured questions)

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/data-visualization#tips-for-effective-data-analysis)

Tips for Effective Data Analysis
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Be specific in your request**:

*   ✅ “Identify seasonal patterns in sales and recommend inventory adjustments”
*   ❌ “Analyze this data”

**Choose appropriate chart types**:

*   Trends over time → Line charts
*   Category comparisons → Bar charts
*   Proportions → Pie charts
*   Correlations → Scatter plots
*   Multi-dimensional → Radar charts

**Select the right output format**:

*   Presenting to executives → Slide deck
*   Ongoing monitoring → Dashboard
*   Documentation → Report
*   External sharing → Webpage

**Provide context in your data**:

*   Include column headers that are self-explanatory
*   Remove unnecessary columns before upload
*   Ensure dates are formatted consistently
*   Clean obvious errors first

**Combine with other Manus features**:

*   Use Wide Research to gather competitive data, then visualize it
*   Create analysis in Data Viz, then embed in Web Development project
*   Generate charts, then include in Slides for comprehensive presentation

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/data-visualization#common-questions)

Common Questions
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

What data formats does Manus accept?

PDF,CSV, Excel (XLSX, XLS), and other common structured data formats. The data should be organized in rows and columns with clear headers for best resultes

Can I analyze multiple datasets at once?

Yes. You can upload multiple files and request analysis that combines or compares them.

How many charts can I create in one analysis?

You can select up to 5 different chart types for a single analysis, ensuring comprehensive visualization of your data.

Can I edit the charts after they're created?

Yes. You can request modifications: “Make the bars wider,” “Change colors to match our brand,” “Add data labels to the pie chart.”

Does Manus handle data cleaning?

Manus can handle basic data preparation, but for best results, ensure your data is reasonably clean before upload. Remove obvious errors and ensure consistent formatting.

Can I export the visualizations?

Yes. Depending on output format, you can export to PowerPoint (slides), PDF (reports), or access standalone webpages with permanent links.

How does this compare to Excel or Google Sheets?

Manus focuses on insight generation and presentation-ready output, not manual data manipulation. It’s faster for creating polished visualizations but not a replacement for detailed spreadsheet work.

Can I use this for real-time dashboards?

The current version works with static datasets. For ongoing monitoring, you can re-run analysis with updated data files.

Access Control

[Introduction](https://manus.im/docs/introduction/welcome)

On this page

*   [Built-in Login System](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/access-control#built-in-login-system)

Manus provides robust access control features to ensure that your application and its content are only accessible to the intended audience. You can secure your entire site or just specific sections, giving you granular control over who sees what.

[​](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/access-control#built-in-login-system)

Built-in Login System
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![Screenshot2025 12 05at10 43 25AM Pn](https://mintcdn.com/docs-manus/EE36eqTNqZEZbTCr/images/Screenshot2025-12-05at10.43.25AM.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=EE36eqTNqZEZbTCr&q=85&s=976d36a23a615d28144953aa8349a3e9) With a simple command, you can add a complete user authentication system to your application. This is essential for creating member-only areas, personalized content, and any feature that requires users to have an account. The built-in system includes:

*   **User Registration**: Allow users to sign up for an account with their email and a password.
*   **Login/Logout**: Securely authenticate users and manage their sessions.
*   **User Management**: View and manage your user base from a central dashboard.

**Example Prompt:**

> “Add a user login and registration system to my site. The login button should be in the top-right corner of the navigation bar.”

[​](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/access-control#role-based-and-individual-permissions)

Role-Based and Individual Permissions
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can restrict access to your entire application or specific pages to certain individuals or teams. This is perfect for building internal tools, client portals, or staging environments.

| Use Case | Description |
| --- | --- |
| **Internal Tools** | Build applications that are only accessible to your team, such as an internal dashboard or a knowledge base. |
| **Client Portals** | Create private, secure areas for your clients to view their project status, access exclusive content, or manage their account. |
| **Staging Environments** | Share a preview of your application with stakeholders for feedback before making it public. |

**Example Prompt:**

> “Make the ‘/admin’ section of this site accessible only to users with the ‘Admin’ role. All other users should be redirected to the homepage.”

# Cloud Infrastructure - Manus Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/cloud-infrastructure#content-area)

Features

Cloud Infrastructure

[Introduction](https://manus.im/docs/introduction/welcome)
[Features](https://manus.im/docs/features/design-view)
[Website Builder](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/getting-started)
[Integrations](https://manus.im/docs/integrations/integrations)

On this page

*   [Backend: The Engine of Your Application](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/cloud-infrastructure#backend%3A-the-engine-of-your-application)
    
*   [Database: Your Application’s Persistent Memory](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/cloud-infrastructure#database%3A-your-application%E2%80%99s-persistent-memory)
    
*   [File Storage: Securely Manage Your Assets](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/cloud-infrastructure#file-storage%3A-securely-manage-your-assets)
    
*   [Deployment: Go Live Instantly](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/cloud-infrastructure#deployment%3A-go-live-instantly)
    

Every web application you build with Manus is powered by a robust and scalable cloud infrastructure, completely managed for you. This means you get the power of a full-stack application without the complexity of managing servers, databases, or deployments. You can focus on building great user experiences, while Manus handles the technical heavy lifting. Here’s a breakdown of the core components and what they enable you to do:

| Component | What It Is | Example Use Cases |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **Backend** | The “brain” of your application that works behind the scenes. | User logins, processing forms, connecting to APIs, custom business logic. |
| **Database** | The “memory” of your application where data is stored permanently. | User profiles, product lists, blog posts, saved settings, form submissions. |
| **File Storage** | The “filing cabinet” for your application’s media and documents. | User-uploaded images, downloadable PDFs, video files, portfolios. |
| **Deployment** | The process of making your application live on the internet. | Publishing your site to a custom domain with a single command. |

* * *

[​](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/cloud-infrastructure#backend:-the-engine-of-your-application)

Backend: The Engine of Your Application
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Unlike traditional website builders that only create a static frontend, Manus builds full-stack applications with a complete backend. This is the crucial server-side component that allows your application to perform actions, remember information, and interact with other services. It’s what makes your site a dynamic web _application_ rather than just a static brochure. With a backend, you can build features that require processing and logic. For example, you can tell Manus:

> “Create a user registration system with email and password authentication.”

> “When a user submits the contact form, save the submission to the database and send me an email notification.”

[​](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/cloud-infrastructure#database:-your-application%E2%80%99s-persistent-memory)

Database: Your Application’s Persistent Memory
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Your application comes with an integrated, persistent database, which acts as its long-term memory. This is where you can store, retrieve, and manage information, allowing your application to grow and evolve. Manus handles all the complex database management tasks like configuration, maintenance, and scaling, so you don’t have to. Use the database to store any kind of structured information. For example:

> “Build a product catalog with fields for name, price, image, and description.”

> “Create a blog and set up a database to store posts, each with a title, author, publication date, and content.”

[​](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/cloud-infrastructure#file-storage:-securely-manage-your-assets)

File Storage: Securely Manage Your Assets
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Manus provides secure and scalable file storage for your application. This allows both you and your users to upload and manage files like images, documents, and other media. It’s essential for creating rich, interactive experiences. This feature is perfect for a wide range of uses. For example:

> “Add a profile picture upload feature to the user account page and store the images securely.”

> “Create a ‘Resources’ page where I can upload and list PDF case studies for users to download.”

[​](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/cloud-infrastructure#deployment:-go-live-instantly)

Deployment: Go Live Instantly
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

With Manus, deploying your application is as simple as giving a command. There are no servers to provision, no deployment scripts to write, and no separate hosting accounts to manage. Manus handles the entire process, ensuring your application is live and accessible to your users in minutes. This unified process means you don’t need to worry about services like AWS, Vercel, or Netlify. It’s all included. For more details on making your site public, see the **Publishing and Collaboration** section.

[Built-in AI Capabilities](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/ai-capabilities)

[​](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/payments#stripe-integration:-effortless-payments)

Stripe Integration: Effortless Payments
======================================================================================================================================

Manus revolutionizes how you integrate payments by partnering with Stripe to offer a “build first, sign up later” workflow. This eliminates the traditional friction of setting up a payments system, allowing you to go from idea to income in a fraction of the time.

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/payments#the-traditional-problem)

The Traditional Problem

Typically, accepting online payments requires a multi-step, technical process: you must first sign up for a payment provider, navigate complex dashboards to configure products and webhooks, build and test your integration, and only then can you deploy your application. This process can take days or even weeks and often requires specialized expertise.

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/payments#the-manus-solution:-build-first,-sign-up-later)

The Manus Solution: Build First, Sign Up Later

Manus flips the traditional model on its head. You can start building your application and integrating payment functionality immediately. The moment you decide to add payments, Manus automatically creates a **Stripe claimable sandbox** for you. This is a temporary, fully-featured Stripe account that requires no initial signup. This approach provides several key advantages:

*   **Zero-Friction Start**: Begin building and testing your payment flows instantly without the barrier of a signup form.
*   **Complete Testing Environment**: The sandbox replicates Stripe’s live environment, allowing you to test your entire checkout process, including subscriptions and payment confirmations, without using real money.
*   **Designed for AI Agents**: This technology allows Manus to securely build and configure your entire payment system on your behalf in a controlled environment.

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/payments#what-manus-handles-automatically)

What Manus Handles Automatically

When you ask Manus to add payments, it acts as your personal payments specialist, handling the complex configuration tasks for you: ![Image(8) Pn](https://mintcdn.com/docs-manus/rKYAjXCWrEKiD9vH/images/image(8).png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=rKYAjXCWrEKiD9vH&q=85&s=4643d7b0786c4364cc53a20a1aa40396)

*   **Automated Product Setup**: Manus translates your business logic into the corresponding products and subscription models in your Stripe sandbox.
*   **Webhook Configuration**: It automatically sets up the necessary webhooks to ensure seamless communication between your application and Stripe for events like successful payments.
*   **End-to-End Testing**: The entire checkout flow is built and tested in the sandbox, ensuring everything works as expected before you go live.

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/payments#step-by-step:-adding-payments)

Step-by-Step: Adding Payments

1.  **Tell Manus Your Goal**: Simply state what you want to sell, for example: `"Add Stripe payments for a premium subscription at $49/month."`
2.  **Manus Sets Up the Sandbox**: Manus will create the claimable sandbox and configure all the necessary products, pricing, and webhooks.
3.  **Test Your Checkout Flow**: You can test the entire payment process in the live preview to ensure everything is working correctly.
4.  **Go Live**: When you are satisfied, tell Manus: `"I'm ready to go live with payments."` You will then be prompted to “claim” the sandbox, which involves creating your official Stripe account and completing their secure Know Your Customer (KYC) process. All the configurations Manus created are seamlessly transferred to your new, permanent Stripe account, ready to accept real payments instantly.

[Notifications](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/notifications)
[Project Analytics](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/project-analytics)

⌘I

Manus-built applications come with integrated analytics, providing you with valuable insights into how users are interacting with your site. This data-driven approach allows you to make informed decisions to improve your application and better serve your audience, all without needing to install or configure third-party tools.

[​](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/project-analytics#built-in-tracking)

Built-in Tracking
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![Screenshot 2025-12-05 at 10.29.52 AM.png](https://mintcdn.com/docs-manus/sz0jlxwOSNUZiwvq/images/Screenshot2025-12-05at10.29.52AM.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=sz0jlxwOSNUZiwvq&q=85&s=b7aa2e01f2332db1d7b4e830898e679e) From the moment your site is live, Manus automatically tracks key metrics, giving you a clear picture of your site’s performance.

| Metric | Description |
| --- | --- |
| **Visitors** | The number of unique users visiting your site over a given period. |
| **Page Views** | The total number of pages viewed, helping you identify your most popular content. |
| **Traffic Sources** | Where your users are coming from, such as direct traffic, search engines, or social media. |
| **Users** | Manus can also show you who your users if they had to log in to access your site |

[​](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/project-analytics#database)

Database
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Every Manus web project with the **database feature** includes a fully managed MySQL database and a visual interface to inspect and manage your data. ![Screenshot 2025-12-05 at 10.29.11 AM.png](https://mintcdn.com/docs-manus/sz0jlxwOSNUZiwvq/images/Screenshot2025-12-05at10.29.11AM.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=sz0jlxwOSNUZiwvq&q=85&s=d0087a847086e220ab9536d8d82c7632)

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/project-analytics#1-visual-data-browser)

**1\. Visual Data Browser**

*   View all tables in your database from the left sidebar
*   Click any table to see its contents in a sortable, searchable grid
*   Inspect individual records by clicking rows

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/project-analytics#2-direct-editing)

**2\. Direct Editing**

*   **Add** new records with the ”+ Add” button
*   **Edit** existing records by clicking cells
*   **Delete** records when needed
*   **Refresh** to see the latest data from your live application

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/project-analytics#3-column-management)

**3\. Column Management**

*   Click “Columns” to view the full schema (data types, constraints, indexes)
*   See which fields are required, unique, or have default values
*   Understand relationships between tables (foreign keys)

Features

Notifications

[Introduction](https://manus.im/docs/introduction/welcome)
[Features](https://manus.im/docs/features/design-view)
[Website Builder](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/getting-started)
[Integrations](https://manus.im/docs/integrations/integrations)

On this page

*   [Setting Up Notifications](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/notifications#setting-up-notifications)
    
*   [Notification Preferences](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/notifications#notification-preferences)
    

Engage your users and stay on top of important activity by setting up automated notifications. Manus allows you to create custom alerts that are triggered by specific events on your website, ensuring you and your users never miss a critical update.

[​](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/notifications#setting-up-notifications)

Setting Up Notifications
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![Screenshot2025 11 24at2 59 00PM Pn](https://mintcdn.com/docs-manus/rKYAjXCWrEKiD9vH/images/Screenshot2025-11-24at2.59.00PM.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=rKYAjXCWrEKiD9vH&q=85&s=4e012fb759a64e8174fa7e43c4488374) Configuring notifications is done conversationally. You simply tell Manus what events you want to be notified about. From the **Settings > Notifications** tab, you can request Manus to set up alerts for any data change on your site. Here are some common examples:

| Notification Trigger | Example Prompt |
| --- | --- |
| **New Form Submission** | `"My website collects user data through a form. Notify me whenever a new form is submitted."` |
| **New Product Sale** | `"My website sells products. Send me a notification every time a new product is sold."` |
| **New Review** | `"My website has a review feature. Alert me immediately when a user leaves a negative review."` |
| **User Sign-up** | `"Send me a notification each time a new user creates an account on my site."` |

[​](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/notifications#notification-preferences)

Notification Preferences
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You have full control over how you receive these alerts. By default, notifications are sent via both email and in-app messages, but you can customize your preferences at any time. Under **Notification Sending Preferences**, you can use the toggles to:

*   **Receive email notifications**: Get alerts sent directly to your inbox.
*   **Receive in-app notifications**: See alerts within the Manus application interface.

You can also download the Manus mobile app to receive push notifications directly on your phone, ensuring you stay connected even when you’re on the go.

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/mail-manus#what-is-mail-manus)

What is Mail Manus?
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Mail Manus is where you can trigger Manus tasks by forwarding emails to a unique bot address. Instead of switching between your inbox and the Manus app, you can delegate work directly from your email client and receive results back via email. This approach integrates Manus into existing email workflows, making it particularly useful for processing incoming emails, handling email-based requests, and automating recurring email tasks without leaving your inbox.

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/mail-manus#how-to-set-up-mail-manus)

How to set up Mail Manus
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**1\. Unique Bot Address**: Each user receives a personal Manus email address (e.g., `[[email protected]](https://manus.im/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection) `) Navigate to Settings → Mail Manus and copy your unique bot email address. ![Mail Manus](https://mintcdn.com/docs-manus/C1PisAhqAuyVufRp/images/mail-manus.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=C1PisAhqAuyVufRp&q=85&s=930d506250b0a69e757429cad238dfed) **2\. Forward or CC**: Forward emails to this address, or CC it in conversations to trigger tasks **3\. Task Processing**: Manus analyzes the email content, attachments, and any instructions you provide **4\. Email Delivery**: Results are sent back to your inbox as email responses, with attachments when applicable **5\. Security**: Only emails from pre-approved sender addresses can trigger tasks

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/mail-manus#advanced-features:-how-to-setup-email-workflows)

Advanced Features: How to setup email workflows
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/mail-manus#workflow-automation)

Workflow Automation

For recurring tasks like travel bookings, expense receipts, or invoice processing, you can set up **workflow emails**—dedicated Manus bot addresses that automatically handle specific types of emails.

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/mail-manus#what-are-workflow-emails)

What are Workflow Emails?

Workflow emails are specialized Manus bot addresses designed for specific recurring tasks. Instead of using your main Mail Manus address, you create purpose-specific addresses like:

*   `[[email protected]](https://manus.im/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection) ` - For flight, hotel, and conference bookings
*   `[[email protected]](https://manus.im/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection) ` - For receipts and expense tracking
*   `[[email protected]](https://manus.im/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection) ` - For invoice processing and logging

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/mail-manus#how-to-set-up-workflow-automation)

How to Set Up Workflow Automation

**Step 1: Create Your Workflow Email** In Manus Settings → Mail Manus → Workflow Emails, create a new workflow email:

Copy

Ask AI

    Name: Business Travel
    Address: [email protected]
    Default Prompt: "Build my itinerary, add check-ins to Calendar, set reminders, and buffer time for travels."
    

**Step 2: Set Up Email Filter** ![Mail Manus](https://mintcdn.com/docs-manus/C1PisAhqAuyVufRp/images/mail-manus2.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=C1PisAhqAuyVufRp&q=85&s=8cc2977779a43cbfd009f665d42ea6ce) In your email client (Gmail/Outlook), create a filter to match specific emails: **Example: Travel Bookings Filter (Gmail)**

Copy

Ask AI

    From: [email protected], [email protected]
    Subject: Business travel
    Includes words: "booking confirmation," "flight," "hotel"
    

**Example: Expense Receipts Filter (Gmail)**

Copy

Ask AI

    From: [email protected]
    Subject: Uber E-Receipt
    

**Step 3: Connect Filter to Workflow Email** Set the filter action to auto-forward matching emails to your workflow email:

Copy

Ask AI

    When message matches criteria:
    ☑ Forward it to: [email protected]
    

**Step 4: Automatic Processing** Once set up, matching emails are automatically:

1.  Forwarded to your workflow email
2.  Processed by Manus using the default prompt
3.  Results sent back to your inbox

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/mail-manus#real-world-workflow-examples)

Real-World Workflow Examples

**Travel Management Workflow**

Copy

Ask AI

    Workflow Email: [email protected]
    Filter: From airlines, hotels, conference organizers
    Default Prompt: "Extract: dates, locations, confirmation numbers.
                    Add to Google Calendar with 1-hour buffer before flights.
                    Set reminders 24h and 2h before departure."
    
    Result: Every booking confirmation automatically becomes calendar events
            with appropriate reminders and travel buffers.
    

**Expense Tracking Workflow**

Copy

Ask AI

    Workflow Email: [email protected]
    Filter: From Uber, Grab, Lyft (receipt emails)
    Default Prompt: "Extract: date, amount, category, merchant.
                    Log to Notion Expenses database."
    
    Result: All ride-sharing receipts automatically logged to expense tracker.
    

**Invoice Processing Workflow**

Copy

Ask AI

    Workflow Email: [email protected]
    Filter: Subject contains "Invoice" + has PDF attachment
    Default Prompt: "Extract: invoice number, date, amount, vendor, due date.
                    Add to Accounting spreadsheet.
                    Set reminder 3 days before due date."
    
    Result: Incoming invoices automatically parsed and tracked with payment reminders.
    

**Customer Feedback Workflow**

Copy

Ask AI

    Workflow Email: [email protected]
    Filter: Subject contains "feedback" or "review"
    Default Prompt: "Analyze sentiment (positive/negative/neutral).
                    Extract key issues and suggestions.
                    Post summary to Slack #customer-feedback channel."
    
    Result: Customer feedback automatically analyzed and shared with team.
    

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/mail-manus#security-and-privacy)

Security and Privacy
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/mail-manus#approved-senders)

Approved Senders

Only emails from pre-approved addresses can trigger Manus tasks. Configure approved senders in Settings → Mail Manus → Approved Senders. **Why**: Prevents unauthorized use of your Manus bot address.

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/mail-manus#email-privacy)

Email Privacy

Manus processes email content to execute tasks. Emails are handled according to Manus’s privacy policy and data handling practices.

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/mail-manus#tips-for-better-results)

Tips for Better Results
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Tip | Good Example | Poor Example |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **Be specific** | ”Create a table with columns: name, company, role, email" | "Organize this” |
| **Provide context** | ”I’m evaluating CRM vendors for our sales team” | \[No context provided\] |
| **Specify format** | ”Generate a slide deck with findings" | "Give me the results” |
| **Use subject line** | Subject: “Extract key dates and deadlines” | \[Blank subject\] |
| **Combine features** | ”Use Wide Research to analyze all 50 items” | \[Single-threaded request\] |

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/mail-manus#when-to-use-mail-manus)

When to Use Mail Manus
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Ideal For**:

*   Processing incoming emails that require research or analysis
*   Converting email threads into structured outputs
*   Automating recurring email-based tasks
*   Delegating work without leaving your inbox
*   Collaborating with team members via email

**Not Ideal For**:

*   Tasks requiring real-time interaction (use Manus app instead)
*   Highly sensitive information (use direct app interface)
*   Tasks requiring immediate results (email has inherent latency)

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/mail-manus#common-questions)

Common Questions
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Is my Mail Manus address private?

Yes. Your bot email address is unique and only processes emails from approved senders.

What types of attachments can Manus process?

PDFs, Word documents, Excel spreadsheets, images, CSVs, and other common formats.

How long does processing take?

Depends on task complexity. Simple summaries take 1-2 minutes; comprehensive research may take 10-15 minutes. Status updates are sent via email.

How long does processing take?

Depends on task complexity. Simple summaries take 1-2 minutes; comprehensive research may take 10-15 minutes. Status updates are sent via email.

Can I cancel a task after forwarding?

Yes. Reply to the status email with “Cancel” or stop the task from the Manus app.

Does Mail Manus use credits?

Yes. Tasks triggered via email consume credits like any other Manus task.

Can I share my Mail Manus address?

No. Each user has a unique address. However, you can CC colleagues in emails to Manus for collaboration.

What happens if I forward something by mistake?

Manus sends a confirmation email before starting complex tasks, allowing you to cancel if needed.

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/mail-manus#)

# Browser Operator - Manus Documentation

[Manus Documentation home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/docs-manus/C1PisAhqAuyVufRp/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=C1PisAhqAuyVufRp&q=85&s=7366a98aefb64c7c37c7dd35d613c640)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/docs-manus/C1PisAhqAuyVufRp/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=C1PisAhqAuyVufRp&q=85&s=1b58c59477c90d5dbf1454f25864b789)](https://manus.im/docs)

*   [FAQ](https://manus.im/docs/features/browser-operator#faq)
    

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/browser-operator#what-it-is)

What it is
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

Manus Browser Operator is a browser extension that transforms your web browser into an autonomous agent. It allows Manus to securely perform tasks on your behalf directly within your local browser, using your existing logins and sessions.

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/browser-operator#true-autonomous-delegation)

True Autonomous Delegation

Manus is a sophisticated AI Agent that doesn’t just chat—it operates. Give it a multi-step goal, and it will plan, navigate, click, and execute the entire workflow across various sites without continuous human supervision.

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/browser-operator#powered-by-your-active-tabs)

Powered by Your Active Tabs

Manus Browser Operator works directly within your current browser session, securely utilizing your existing logins and active tabs to complete tasks on sites you already use and trust.

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/browser-operator#automate-your-most-tedious-tasks)

Automate Your Most Tedious Tasks

Instantly eliminate manual clicking, form filling, and cross-platform data extraction. From complex research and booking logistics to summarizing data, Manus handles the tedious processes that take hours out of your day.

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/browser-operator#how-to-use-it)

How to use it
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/browser-operator#1-connect-browser)

1\. Connect Browser

![Connect Browser](https://mintcdn.com/docs-manus/bQkH44IdiITg8-s-/images/connectbrowser.webp?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=bQkH44IdiITg8-s-&q=85&s=d449143bac7d9ca39c615b4f7ebe8f09 "Connect Browser") Enable the **Manus Browser Operator** in the Manus **Connectors** tab. A browser extension will be installed to link Manus with your browser.

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/browser-operator#2-grant-access)

2\. Grant Access

![Use Browser](https://mintcdn.com/docs-manus/bQkH44IdiITg8-s-/images/usebrowser.webp?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=bQkH44IdiITg8-s-&q=85&s=d68092a3169c0e09adf0f4102920150b "Use Browser") When you assign a task requiring web access, Manus will ask for permission to control your browser. Grant access to allow the agent to take over.

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/browser-operator#3-autonomous-action)

3\. Autonomous Action

Manus works in a dedicated tab to complete your task. It uses your logged-in sessions to navigate websites, gather information, and perform actions as instructed.

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/browser-operator#what-you-need-to-know)

What you need to know
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/browser-operator#local-vs-cloud-browser)

Local vs. Cloud Browser

The Browser Operator uses your **local browser**, which is ideal for tasks requiring access to sites where you are already logged in. This avoids CAPTCHAs and security checks. For other tasks, Manus uses an isolated **Cloud Browser**.

| Feature | Manus Browser Operator (Local) | Cloud Browser |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **Environment** | Your local desktop browser | Isolated, sandboxed cloud environment |
| **Authentication** | Uses your existing browser logins | Requires logging in within the session |
| **Best For** | Authenticated sessions, sensitive sites | General web tasks, broad research |

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/browser-operator#security-and-control)

Security and Control

You have full control over the Browser Operator. You must authorize every session, and you can stop the agent at any time by simply closing the browser tab. All actions are logged for complete transparency.

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/browser-operator#tips)

Tips
-----------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Use for Authenticated Sites:** Best for tasks on sites like LinkedIn, CRMs, or premium tools you are already logged into.
*   **Be Specific:** Give clear, step-by-step instructions for the best results.
*   **Monitor Complex Tasks:** Keep an eye on the dedicated browser tab for multi-step workflows to ensure they run smoothly.

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/browser-operator#faq)

FAQ
---------------------------------------------------------------

Is it secure?

You authorize each session and can stop it at any time. All actions are logged, and Manus never stores your passwords.

What browsers are supported?

Chrome and Edge are currently recommended. Support for other browsers is coming soon

Can I use it on mobile?

You can start and monitor tasks from mobile, but the Operator runs on your desktop browser, which must be online.

What if a task goes wrong?

A: You can take over by clicking into the tab or stop the task completely by closing the tab.

[Cloud browser](https://manus.im/docs/features/cloud-browser)

⌘I

Manus works with multiple media types—generating images, understanding video content, creating voice output, and transcribing speech. Combine text, images, video, and audio in your workflows seamlessly.

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/multi-modal#capabilities-overview)

Capabilities Overview
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Capability | What It Does | Example Use |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **Image Generation** | Create custom images from descriptions | Product mockups, illustrations, diagrams |
| **Image Understanding** | Analyze and extract info from images | Document scanning, visual analysis |
| **Video Understanding** | Analyze video content and extract insights | Meeting transcripts, content analysis |
| **Voice Output** | Convert text to natural speech | Voiceovers, audio content |
| **Speech to Text** | Transcribe audio to text | Meeting notes, interview transcripts |

Tips for Better Images

**Be specific about style**:

*   ✅ “Minimalist, modern, professional photography”
*   ✅ “Flat design illustration, bright colors”
*   ❌ “Make it look good”

**Describe composition**:

*   ✅ “Centered subject, blurred background, natural lighting”
*   ❌ “A picture of…”

**Specify use case**:

*   ✅ “For Instagram post, square format, bold text overlay”
*   ✅ “For presentation slide, wide format, subtle background”

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/multi-modal#common-questions)

Common Questions
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**What image formats are supported?** PNG, JPG, WEBP, GIF, and more. For generation, you can specify format. **How long can videos be?** Manus can process videos up to several hours long. Longer videos take more time. **What audio formats work for transcription?** MP3, WAV, M4A, WEBM, and most common audio formats. **Can I generate images in specific sizes?** Yes. Specify dimensions: “Generate a 1920x1080 image…” or “Square format for Instagram…” **How accurate is speech transcription?** Very high accuracy, even with accents, multiple speakers, or background noise. **Can I generate videos?** Yes. Manus can generate short video clips and animations. **Are there limits on generation?** Generation uses credits. Check your plan for limits.

* * *

[​](https://manus.im/docs/features/multi-modal#quick-use-cases)

Quick Use Cases
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Use Case | Input | Output |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **Product Mockups** | Description | Generated images |
| **Meeting Notes** | Video recording | Transcript + summary |
| **Blog Audio** | Text article | Audio narration |
| **Document Scanning** | Photo of document | Extracted text |
| **Video Analysis** | Competitor video | Feature comparison |
| **Podcast Show Notes** | Audio file | Transcript + summary |
| **Social Graphics** | Description | Custom images |

* * *

**Bottom line**: Manus handles multiple media types seamlessly. Generate images, understand video, create voice output, and transcribe speech—all integrated into your workflows.

Developer Tools

Code Control

[Introduction](https://manus.im/docs/introduction/welcome)
[Features](https://manus.im/docs/features/design-view)
[Website Builder](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/getting-started)
[Integrations](https://manus.im/docs/integrations/integrations)

On this page

*   [Copy](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/code-control#copy)
    
*   [Download](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/code-control#download)
    

While Manus allows you to build and manage your entire web application without writing a single line of code, it also provides full access to the underlying code for those who want it. This ensures that you are never locked into the platform and have complete control over your application.

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/code-control#copy)

Copy

You can copy snippets of code directly from the interface. This is useful if you want to inspect a specific component or reuse a piece of code in another project.

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/code-control#download)

Download

For complete control, you can download the entire codebase for your application at any time. This gives you a complete copy of all the frontend and backend files, allowing you to:

*   **Move to Your Own Hosting**: You can take the code and host it on any server or platform of your choice.
*   **Customize and Extend**: If you have development experience, you can modify the code to add custom features or make advanced modifications.
*   **Integrate with Your Own Workflow**: You can integrate the code into your existing development workflow, such as a Git repository or a CI/CD pipeline.

This commitment to code transparency and portability ensures that you always have the flexibility to adapt and grow your application as your needs evolve.

# Third-Party Integrations - Manus Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/third-party-integrations#content-area)

[Manus Documentation home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/docs-manus/C1PisAhqAuyVufRp/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=C1PisAhqAuyVufRp&q=85&s=7366a98aefb64c7c37c7dd35d613c640)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/docs-manus/C1PisAhqAuyVufRp/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=C1PisAhqAuyVufRp&q=85&s=1b58c59477c90d5dbf1454f25864b789)](https://manus.im/docs)

Navigation

Developer Tools

Third-Party Integrations

[Introduction](https://manus.im/docs/introduction/welcome)
[Features](https://manus.im/docs/features/design-view)
[Website Builder](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/getting-started)
[Integrations](https://manus.im/docs/integrations/integrations)

On this page

*   [Stripe](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/third-party-integrations#stripe)
    
*   [Google Maps](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/third-party-integrations#google-maps)
    
*   [Custom API](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/third-party-integrations#custom-api)
    
*   [API Secrets: Securely Manage Your Keys](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/third-party-integrations#api-secrets%3A-securely-manage-your-keys)
    
*   [Adding API Secret key](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/third-party-integrations#adding-api-secret-key)
    

Manus allows you to extend the functionality of your web application by integrating with a variety of third-party services. This enables you to build more powerful and feature-rich applications without leaving the conversational interface.

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/third-party-integrations#stripe)

Stripe

Integrate a complete, secure, and production-ready payment system with Stripe. Manus handles the entire process, from creating products and subscription models to configuring webhooks and testing the checkout flow. For more details, see the dedicated “[Payments](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/payments)
” section.

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/third-party-integrations#google-maps)

Google Maps

Incorporate location-based features into your application with Google Maps. You can:

*   Display interactive maps.
*   Show the location of your business or points of interest.
*   Build features like store locators or delivery tracking.

To add a map, simply describe where you want it and what it should display, for example:

> “Add a Google Map to the contact page showing our office location at 1600 Amphitheatre Parkway, Mountain View, CA.”

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/third-party-integrations#custom-api)

Custom API

Connect to any third-party service with a REST API to pull in external data or trigger actions in other systems. Manus can handle the authentication and make requests to the API on your behalf. To set up a custom integration, you will need to provide the API endpoint, authentication details (such as an API key), and a description of the data you want to access or the actions you want to perform.

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/third-party-integrations#api-secrets:-securely-manage-your-keys)

API Secrets: Securely Manage Your Keys

When integrating with third-party services, such as Google Maps or a custom API, you will often need to use API keys or other secrets to authenticate your requests. Manus provides a secure way to manage these secrets, ensuring they are not exposed in your frontend code.

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/third-party-integrations#adding-api-secret-key)

Adding API Secret key

You can add API secret key to your project by providing them to Manus in the conversational interface. Manus will store these secret key securely and use them to make authenticated requests on your behalf from the backend. For example, when setting up a custom API integration, you might say:

> “I need to connect to a custom API. The API key is YOUR\_API\_KEY. Please use this key in the Authorization header for all requests.”

Manus will store the API key as an environment variable on the server and will not expose it in the client-side code. This ensures that your secrets remain confidential and your application is secure.

[Import from Figma: From Design to App in One Step](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/import-figma)
[Github Integration](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/github-integration)

# Custom Domains: Professionalize Your Brand - Manus Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/custom-domains#content-area)

[Manus Documentation home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/docs-manus/C1PisAhqAuyVufRp/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=C1PisAhqAuyVufRp&q=85&s=7366a98aefb64c7c37c7dd35d613c640)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/docs-manus/C1PisAhqAuyVufRp/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=C1PisAhqAuyVufRp&q=85&s=1b58c59477c90d5dbf1454f25864b789)](https://manus.im/docs)

![US](https://d3gk2c5xim1je2.cloudfront.net/flags/US.svg)

English

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Project Management

Custom Domains: Professionalize Your Brand

[Introduction](https://manus.im/docs/introduction/welcome)
[Features](https://manus.im/docs/features/design-view)
[Website Builder](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/getting-started)
[Integrations](https://manus.im/docs/integrations/integrations)

On this page

*   [Connecting Your Domain](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/custom-domains#connecting-your-domain)
    
*   [Purchasing a Domain](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/custom-domains#purchasing-a-domain)
    
*   [Automatic SSL/HTTPS](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/custom-domains#automatic-ssl%2Fhttps)
    

A real product deserves a real address. Manus now lets you connect or purchase a custom domain directly inside the builder—no Namecheap detours, no DNS guesswork, no broken onboarding flow. You choose the domain, we handle the setup.

Give your web application a professional and memorable address by connecting your own custom domain. Manus makes it easy to publish your site to any domain or subdomain that you own.

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/custom-domains#connecting-your-domain)

Connecting Your Domain

To connect your domain, you simply need to tell Manus which domain you want to use. For example:

> “Publish this site to my custom domain, [www.example.com](http://www.example.com/)
> .”

Manus will then provide you with the necessary DNS records that you will need to add to your domain registrar’s settings. This typically involves adding or updating an A record or a CNAME record.

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/custom-domains#purchasing-a-domain)

Purchasing a Domain

Purchasing a custom domain inside Manus is now one of the fastest steps in going live. Instead of bouncing between external registrars and juggling DNS settings, you can search, buy, and secure your domain directly within the builder. Everything updates on the same page, and Manus handles the setup behind the scenes. This means you can move from prototype to a fully branded, public site in minutes. Whether you are launching your first product or taking an existing project live, buying your domain through Manus keeps the entire process simple, consistent, and fast.

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/custom-domains#automatic-ssl/https)

Automatic SSL/HTTPS

Security is handled automatically. Once your domain is connected, Manus will provision and configure a free SSL/TLS certificate for your site. This ensures that all traffic to and from your application is encrypted, providing a secure experience for your users and improving your site’s search engine ranking.

[Project Analytics](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/project-analytics)
 [Search Engine Optimization](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/seo)

# Import from Figma: From Design to App in One Step - Manus Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/import-figma#content-area)

[Manus Documentation home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/docs-manus/C1PisAhqAuyVufRp/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=C1PisAhqAuyVufRp&q=85&s=7366a98aefb64c7c37c7dd35d613c640)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/docs-manus/C1PisAhqAuyVufRp/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=C1PisAhqAuyVufRp&q=85&s=1b58c59477c90d5dbf1454f25864b789)](https://manus.im/docs)

![US](https://d3gk2c5xim1je2.cloudfront.net/flags/US.svg)

English

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Developer Tools

Import from Figma: From Design to App in One Step

[Introduction](https://manus.im/docs/introduction/welcome)
[Features](https://manus.im/docs/features/design-view)
[Website Builder](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/getting-started)
[Integrations](https://manus.im/docs/integrations/integrations)

On this page

*   [How It Works](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/import-figma#how-it-works)
    
*   [The Process](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/import-figma#the-process)
    

For teams that use Figma for their design process, Manus offers a powerful integration that allows you to turn your designs into functional web applications with a single command.

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/import-figma#how-it-works)

How It Works

Instead of manually translating your Figma designs into code, you can simply provide Manus with a link to your Figma file. Manus will analyze the design, including the layouts, components, fonts, and colors, and automatically generate the corresponding code for a web application.

### 

[​](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/import-figma#the-process)

The Process

1.  **Design in Figma**: Create your application design in Figma as you normally would. ![image.png](https://mintcdn.com/docs-manus/lidNm1_-GLX2OqHW/images/image.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=lidNm1_-GLX2OqHW&q=85&s=7c31ffba568e37ff14eaa56e6b2f0784)
2.  **Provide the Link**: Share the Figma frame link with Manus and describe what you want to build. For example:
    
    > “Here is the Figma design for our new mobile app. Build a functional web application based on this design.”
    
3.  **Manus Builds the App**: Manus will interpret the design and generate the HTML, CSS, and JavaScript for the frontend, as well as the necessary backend components to bring your design to life.
    
    You can attach multiple frames to your request. Tell Manus how these frames relate—page flow, interactions, or component states (like hover). This helps Manus generate accurate multi-page or interactive experiences.
    

This integration dramatically accelerates the development process, bridging the gap between design and development and allowing you to go from a static design to a live, interactive application in a fraction of the time.

[Code Control](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/code-control)
[Third-Party Integrations](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/third-party-integrations)

⌘I

# Search Engine Optimization - Manus Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/seo#content-area)

Project Management

Search Engine Optimization

[Introduction](https://manus.im/docs/introduction/welcome)
[Features](https://manus.im/docs/features/design-view)
[Website Builder](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/getting-started)
[Integrations](https://manus.im/docs/integrations/integrations)

On this page

*   [How to Use It](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/seo#how-to-use-it)
    
*   [What You Need to Know](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/seo#what-you-need-to-know)
    
*   [Tips](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/seo#tips)
    
*   [FAQ](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/seo#faq)
    

The built-in SEO feature in Manus is a powerful tool designed to improve your web app’s visibility on search engines like Google. It automatically makes your Manus-built websites more search-engine-friendly, helping you attract more organic traffic. The system works by generating a prerendered, static HTML version of your site specifically for search engine bots. This ensures that your content can be easily crawled, indexed, and ranked, while your human visitors continue to enjoy the rich, interactive experience you designed.

[​](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/seo#how-to-use-it)

How to Use It
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

![Screenshot 2025 12 19 At 5 42 00 PM](https://mintcdn.com/docs-manus/LmMcVFND8sHcaCYN/images/Screenshot2025-12-19at5.42.00PM.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=LmMcVFND8sHcaCYN&q=85&s=850f5b761169f296b92c0787917b2e22) Optimizing your site for search engines is a straightforward process with Manus. Follow these steps to get started:

1.  **Enable SEO:** Navigate to your project’s Settings, publish your site, and toggle on the SEO feature. This will initiate the automatic prerendering process.
2.  **Check Your Score:** Go to the SEO tab in your project dashboard. Here, you’ll find a real-time health score for your page and a checklist of important SEO metrics.
3.  **Fix with AI:** Instead of manually fixing these issues, you can use the “Optimize with Manus” button. This AI-powered feature will analyze your page content and automatically generate optimized titles, descriptions, and keywords for you.
4.  **Identify Issues:** The SEO dashboard will highlight any issues. These might include missing meta descriptions, a lack of keywords, or other on-page SEO problems.
5.  \*\*Verify & Rank: \*\*Once the optimizations are applied, you’ll see your SEO score improve. Your site is now technically optimized for search engine crawlers.

![Screenshot 2025 12 19 At 5 42 27 PM](https://mintcdn.com/docs-manus/LmMcVFND8sHcaCYN/images/Screenshot2025-12-19at5.42.27PM.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=LmMcVFND8sHcaCYN&q=85&s=233a9129c05c03a813867c8e41b42871)

[​](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/seo#what-you-need-to-know)

What You Need to Know
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Our built-in SEO feature comes with several key capabilities to help you succeed:

*   Automatic Prerendering: Manus automatically serves a lightweight, fully-optimized HTML version of your site to all major search engine bots, ensuring proper indexing.
*   Automated Technical SEO: The system handles critical technical SEO tasks automatically, such as generating canonical URLs, creating a robots.txt file, and maintaining dynamic sitemaps.
*   SEO Analysis & Scoring: The SEO dashboard provides a detailed health check for every page, scoring your on-page SEO and offering actionable recommendations.
*   AI-Powered Optimization: The “Optimize with Manus” feature uses AI to automatically implement the dashboard’s recommendations, saving you time and effort.

This advanced SEO feature is available as an exclusive benefit for all Manus Members on paid subscription plans.

[​](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/seo#tips)

Tips
-----------------------------------------------------------

To get the most out of our SEO feature, consider the following tips:

*   Submit Your Sitemap: While not strictly required, submitting your sitemap to Google Search Console can significantly speed up the discovery and indexing of your site.
*   Use a Custom Domain: A custom domain can improve your branding and may contribute to better SEO performance.
*   Regularly Monitor Your SEO Score: Keep an eye on your SEO dashboard for new recommendations and opportunities for improvement.

[​](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/seo#faq)

FAQ
---------------------------------------------------------

Do I need to be an SEO expert to use this?

Not at all. These features are designed to automate the most complex technical aspects of SEO, so you can improve your ranking without being an expert. The dashboard provides simple, clear guidance, and the AI-powered “Optimize with Manus” feature can handle the implementation for you.

How does this affect my site's performance for regular visitors?

It doesn’t. The prerendered version of your site is only served to search engine bots. Your human visitors will continue to experience the fast, dynamic version of your site exactly as you designed it.

What if I don’t want my site to be indexed?

Manus does not currently support a “Private Publish” option. However, without enabling SEO optimization, your site will be much harder for search engines to discover and index effectively. For restricted access, you can share your project via email with specific visitors or publish it within your team.

[Custom Domains: Professionalize Your Brand](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/custom-domains)
[Code Control](https://manus.im/docs/website-builder/code-control)
